🧠 Project Recap
Hi ChatGPT — I’m working on a Python-based SOC Access Management Tool for Marchex’s internal SOC team. It’s designed to manage user access across internal systems via both a CLI and Tkinter GUI frontend, with LDAP authentication and audit logging.

Here's where the project currently stands:

✅ Project Goals
Allow SOC analysts to check, grant, and remove user access to internal systems.

Support both interactive CLI and GUI (Tkinter/X11) usage.

Require LDAP authentication before actions are allowed.

Include RT ticketing integration and mock mode for testing.

Be simple, portable, and self-contained — no unnecessary complexity like external microservices or modules.

📁 Current Code Structure
soctool.py – Tkinter GUI wrapper.

access_management.py – CLI backend for access operations (handles all business logic).

Utils/get_secrets.py – Loads secrets from a local JSON file.

Utils/rt_api.py – (Optional) for writing comments to RT tickets.

Systems/UIs/ – Folder of individual check/grant/remove scripts per system (e.g., check_jira.py, remove_grafana.py, etc.).

Logs/ – Centralized log storage for all actions.

🛠️ Progress So Far
✔️ Full project moved to the SOC1 workstation VM.

✔️ GUI works via PuTTY + Xming with X11 forwarding.

✔️ .gitignore updated; changes pushed to repo from VM.

✔️ GUI now defers LDAP auth to access_management.py.

✔️ CLI now accepts --ldap_user and --ldap_pass args.

✔️ LDAP auth logic attempts SIMPLE bind with UPN (username@marchex.com) to ldaps://ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com:636.

✔️ Debug logging added to CLI and GUI.

🧪 Current Blocking Issue
LDAP auth consistently fails with:

yaml
Copy
Edit
LDAP auth failed: invalidDNSyntax
LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.
This happens even when formatting usernames as username@marchex.com.

The bind is attempted to the correct OCI-based server (ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com) over LDAPS with port 636.

We've verified that the credentials are correct, but the syntax or auth method might still be off.

May need to try domain-style (marchex\\username) or full DN formats.

Possibly requires environment-specific configuration or escalation to Infra/IT for exact bind rules.

🔜 Next Steps
Run access_management.py manually with hardcoded credentials to isolate issues.

Trial multiple user formats for the bind:

username@marchex.com

marchex\\username

cn=User Name,dc=marchex,dc=com

Confirm if LDAPS server supports SIMPLE auth with UPN or requires NTLM/domain.

Finalize mock mode and RT ticket integration.

Package tool with README/setup instructions once auth is resolved.

Here’s the current status of my project. Please help me troubleshoot or continue working from this point.

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import getpass
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core, SIMPLE
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "UIs")  # Locate Systems/UIs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

required_keys = ["_JIRA_API_KEY", "_GRAFANA_API_KEY"]
for key in required_keys:
    if not get_secret(key):
        print(f"⚠️ Missing required secret: {key}")
        sys.exit(1)


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")

from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, SIMPLE, ALL

def try_bind(user_format, password, auth_type):
    server = Server('ldaps://ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com', port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
    try:
        conn = Connection(server, user=user_format, password=password, authentication=auth_type)
        if conn.bind():
            print(f"[SUCCESS] {auth_type} bind with user='{user_format}'")
        else:
            print(f"[FAILURE] {auth_type} bind with user='{user_format}' — {conn.result}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] {auth_type} bind with user='{user_format}' — {e}")

# Test combinations
try_bind("marchex\\yourusername", "yourpassword", NTLM)
try_bind("username@marchex.com", "yourpassword", SIMPLE)
try_bind("cn=Your Name,ou=Users,dc=marchex,dc=com", "yourpassword", SIMPLE)


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com"
    try:
        # Enforce full UPN format if not already provided
        if "@" not in username:
            username = f"{username}@marchex.com"

        print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as: {username} to {ldap_server}")

        # Use proper server setup
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)

        # Explicitly use SIMPLE auth
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=username,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}")
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {username}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}")
        return False





# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        print("❌ Error: 'Systems/UIs' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        sys.exit(1)


    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith("check_"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"remove_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"grant_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Main interactive workflow
def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap():
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)
I got a response from Tim about ldap authentication 
I asked if the ldap sever supports SIMPLE bind with UPNs, or requires full DN?

He said 

"Neither our eDirectory nor our OpenLDAP servers support userPrincipalName. That's generally a AD attribute (similar to sAMAccountName). That said, both of those directories at Marchex DO support SIMPLE authentication, but they require the full DN. To illustrate, here's a typical non-anonymous ldapsearch command at Marchex. ldapsearch -xvWD 'uid=kboller,ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com' -LLL -H ldaps://ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com -b 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com' '(uid=kboller)' man ldapsearch will explain all of those options in more details, but suffice it to say that's a SIMPLE auth with full DN & prompting for password instead of taking it on the CLI. One last note: That's for the OpenLDAP servers (which will have ldap in their name). To bind to the eDirectory servers (which I generally try to disuade folks from doing because they're not really meant to be searched by clients), the DN is built from cn instead of uid. The rest of the DN is identical.
Now...if you don't have to bind to a user object, we also support anonymous binding. Just remove the -WD $dn part of the command above.
Anonymous binding will get you just about as much data as you'd need for normal informational operations (like finding out from which groups a user object needs to be removed). If you're wanting to authenticate an application against a user object (effectively requiring binding to get deeper into the app) or make any changes to the directory, you'll need to bind to a user object.
Let me know if anything's unclear or if you have additional questions. I'm happy to answer them (though my Teams notifications are off after 1800 daily so I'll likely respond tomorrow).
And if this IS for your separation script, that's an instance where I think querying eDirectory is a fine time to do it.
It's our source of truth for proper LDAP accounts (AD being the ultimate source of truth for Marchex accounts).
Clear as mud?"

from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, SIMPLE, ALL

def try_bind(user_format, password, auth_type):
    server = Server('ldaps://ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com', port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
    try:
        conn = Connection(server, user=user_format, password=password, authentication=auth_type)
        if conn.bind():
            print(f"[SUCCESS] {auth_type} bind with user='{user_format}'")
        else:
            print(f"[FAILURE] {auth_type} bind with user='{user_format}' — {conn.result}")

def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}")

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}")
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}")
        return False

and heres my get_secrets.py file

import json
import os
import logging

SECRETS_FILE = os.environ.get("SOC_SECRET_FILE", os.path.expanduser("~/soc-secrets/creds.json"))

def get_secret(key):
    """Retrieve secret from local JSON file."""
    try:
        with open(SECRETS_FILE, 'r') as f:
            secrets = json.load(f)
        return secrets.get(key)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Secrets file not found at {SECRETS_FILE}")
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        logging.error("❌ Secrets file is not valid JSON.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error loading secret '{key}': {e}")
    return None


lets go thru each of the system scripts alphabetically and see how we may need to modify each one to log a soc user into each system by using the creds.json file. below is the adtrack.py script




# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import sys
from azure.identity import DefaultAzureCredential
from azure.keyvault.secrets import SecretClient

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Azure Key Vault Configuration
KEY_VAULT_NAME = "soc-prd-eus-access-kv"  # Change as needed
KEY_VAULT_URL = f"https://{KEY_VAULT_NAME}.vault.azure.net"

# ✅ Initialize Azure Key Vault Client
try:
    credential = DefaultAzureCredential()
    client = SecretClient(vault_url=KEY_VAULT_URL, credential=credential)
    
    # ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Azure Key Vault
    ADTRACK_DB_USER = client.get_secret("AdTrack-DB-User").value
    ADTRACK_DB_PASS = client.get_secret("AdTrack-DB-Password").value

except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve secrets from Azure Key Vault: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)  # Exit if credentials cannot be retrieved

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grant AdTrack access to a user based on the SOP."""
    
    # 🚨 FUTURE TASK: Implement UI automation to handle this (e.g., Selenium, API, or Web Scraping)
    logging.info(f"🚀 Granting access to {user} ({real_name}) in AdTrack...")

    # Steps per SOP:
    # 1. Log in with stored credentials (done via Azure Key Vault)
    # 2. Create user in "Marchex Voice Services" group
    # 3. If "staff level" is required, assign permissions accordingly
    # 4. Generate password and send to user (currently not automated)

    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted AdTrack UI access to {user}.")

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user):
    """Remove AdTrack access per SOP."""
    
    logging.info(f"🚀 Removing access for {user} from AdTrack...")

    # Steps per SOP:
    # 1. Log into AdTrack UI
    # 2. Search for user by email
    # 3. Set account status to 'disabled'

    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully disabled AdTrack UI access for {user}.")

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    """Manage AdTrack UI access."""
    
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = input("Enter LDAP user to check: ").strip()
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

heres the SOC SOP for AdTrack UI Access





SOC SOP uiAccessAdTrack
SOC SOP uiAccessAdTrack
Jump to navigationJump to search

Contents
1	Description
2	Adding Access
2.1	If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
2.1.1	NOTE
3	Removing Access
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the Adtrack UI, aka Marchex.IO

Adding AccessRemoving Access

When an account needs to be added by request/ticket use the following steps.


If a user requests access to the Adtrack UI also called Marchex.io and need access to the tool. Most of our requests are for "staff level" access. See "Adtrack Account standards" link below

Adtrack Account standards 
If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_adtrackUIAccountStandards

1. Log into Adtrack

Service Account & Password found in Bitwarden

2. Click the Client List tab in the UI.

3. Unless specified in the ticket create their account in the following group:

Marchex Voice Services (nee Voicestar) (This has been the historic place to put accounts for Marchex users.)

Note:

Sometimes you will have to match an account with another account.
The easiest way to do that is to open a two tabs in your browser.
In the first one, search in "Client list" using the target email (user to copy)
Then follow the below steps and just match up all the permissions.
4. Click on the Account Name, it will drop down, and click Account Settings.

5. Click Users

6. Click "New user".

7. Fill in the user's information:

Real Name
Email
Password [Password Gen]
NOTE:

If the email account is already in use, the tool will not let you use it again. You either have to alter the email with a Capital letter or find the other account and update that one.

8. Click submit at the bottom.

9. Search for the users account once more to provision it.

10. Using either given credentials from another account (Not preferred method) or [staff level] provision the account and click "update" at the bottom.

There are three specific pieces that Require more than the users manager approval: Bulk create /update Campaigns & accounts, Billing Write , and Edit Staff Permissions . See above staff level link.

11. Email the credentials to the user.


NOTE
Adtrack staff tools exist Here and will soon (hopefully) have a staff search function, at which point the above instructions will be thankfully obsolete.

Removing Access

When an account needs to be removed either from a separation or SOX audit or team change use the following steps.


1. Log onto [AdtrackUI/Marchex.io]

Service Account & Password found in Keypass

2. Click on "Client List"

3. In the top right enter the email address of the user you wish to remove.

This will return account groups with the email addresses in the users.

4. For all account groups found, perform the following:

Click on the account, it will drop down. click Account Settings
Click Users
Search again in the top right corner for the user's email address
Click on the correct user
Click User Settings
Set the status to disabled
Click Update
im not sure what Selenium or Playwright is but all were looking to do with the Adtrack.py script is to just be able to grant, revoke or check an ldap users access

import logging

)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grant AdTrack access to a user based on the SOP."""
    
    # 🚨 FUTURE TASK: Implement UI automation to handle this (e.g., Selenium, API, or Web Scraping)
    logging.info(f"🚀 Granting access to {user} ({real_name}) in AdTrack...")

    # Steps per SOP:
    # 1. Log in with stored credentials (done via Azure Key Vault)
    # 2. Create user in "Marchex Voice Services" group
    # 3. If "staff level" is required, assign permissions accordingly
    # 4. Generate password and send to user (currently not automated)

    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted AdTrack UI access to {user}.")

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user):
    """Remove AdTrack access per SOP."""
    
    logging.info(f"🚀 Removing access for {user} from AdTrack...")

    # Steps per SOP:
    # 1. Log into AdTrack UI
    # 2. Search for user by email
    # 3. Set account status to 'disabled'

    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully disabled AdTrack UI access for {user}.")

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import getpass
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core, SIMPLE
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "UIs")  # Locate Systems/UIs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")

required_keys = ["_JIRA_API_KEY", "_GRAFANA_API_KEY"]
for key in required_keys:
    if not get_secret(key):
        print(f"⚠️ Missing required secret: {key}")
        sys.exit(1)


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}")

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}")
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}")
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        print("❌ Error: 'Systems/UIs' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        sys.exit(1)


    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py") and script.startswith("check_"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"remove_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"grant_{system_name.lower()}.py")

    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")

        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)
i no longer have check_*.py, grant_*.py, etc. for each system, i have refactored that for each system to only have one script that does all 3 functions for that system so instead of check_adtrack, grant_adtrack and remove_ adtrack i just have one adtrack.py script that does all 3 things.
"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).

#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345

LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}")

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}")
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}")
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    if not os.path.exists(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        print("❌ Error: 'Systems/UIs' directory not found.")
        logging.error("Systems directory missing.")
        sys.exit(1)


    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, "check", target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, target_user]
                process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                if stdout_output.strip():
                    print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                    access_list.append(system_name)

                if stderr_output.strip():
                    print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                    logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    return access_list

# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Removes access from the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, "remove", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    """Grants access to the selected system."""
    script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
    if os.path.exists(script_path):
        cmd = ["python", script_path, "grant", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")

def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)




so when the SOC user of the tool inputs thier ldap username and password and the target users ldap username the access_management script should search thru each system for that target user and provide a list of what systems that target user currently has access too

# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import sys
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            # Example insert — customize based on your DB schema
            cur.execute("""
                INSERT INTO at_user (email, name, status, staff_level)
                VALUES (%s, %s, 'active', %s)
                ON CONFLICT (email) DO UPDATE SET status = 'active'
            """, (user_email, real_name, 'staff' if is_staff else 'user'))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant access to {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Grant failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    found_any = False

    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        if not os.path.exists(directory):
            continue  # silently skip missing dirs

        found_any = True

        for script in os.listdir(directory):
            if script.endswith(".py"):
                system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
                script_path = os.path.join(directory, script)

                try:
                    cmd = ["python", script_path, "check", target_user]
                    process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                    stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                    if stdout_output.strip():
                        print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                        access_list.append(system_name)

                    if stderr_output.strip():
                        print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                        logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                    logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    if not found_any:
        print("❌ Error: No valid system directories found (expected Systems/UIs or Systems/DBs).")
        logging.error("No system directories found.")

    return access_list


def find_script(system_name):
    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        script_path = os.path.join(directory, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            return script_path
    return None


# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = ["python", script_path, "remove", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")

        
# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = ["python", script_path, "grant", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")


def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)

Frequently asked questions
How do I connect to OpenVPN?
In order to connect to the VPN server or service, you need to obtain a file that contains the specifics needed for the connection. Such a configuration file is called a profile and has an .ovpn file extension.

If your business is using Access Server or CloudConnexa and your IT department has provided you a URL, you can directly import the profile by entering the URL.



However, if you have received the profile as a file from your IT department or from some other OpenVPN compatible service, you can import the profile by selecting the file.



How do I connect if the OpenVPN client is integrated into my router?
In order to connect to the VPN server or service, you need to obtain a file that contains the specifics needed for the connection. Such a configuration file is called a profile and has an .ovpn file extension.

After receiving the .ovpn file from you IT department, you need to follow instructions specific to the router to extract specific information from the file and use it for configuration. We have made guides for some of the common firmware used in hardware routers and for pfSense:

pfSense

OpenWrt

DD-WRT

📘 SOC Access Management – Knowledge Transfer (KT)
🗂️ Repo: marchex-emu/socbot – restructuring branch 

Author: Ken Boller
Last Updated: March 17th 2025
Audience: SOC Engineering, DevOps, Security

This document provides a full overview of the SOC Access Management project — including file structure, systems integrated, scripts updated/created, and how to test or run the project in production. It also outlines what's been completed, what remains, and how to maintain/extend the toolset during the author’s leave.

🧭 Project Overview
The SOC Access Management Toolkit allows the Security Operations Center (SOC) to manage user access across 20+ internal systems using a unified process:

✅ CLI Tool (access_management.py)
✅ GUI Wrapper (soctool.py)
✅ Modular per-system scripts (located in Systems/UIs/ and Systems/DBs/)
🔐 Credential integration pending (via SOC Cloud Workstation)

# 📘 SOC Access Management – Knowledge Transfer (KT)
🗂️ **Repo**: [marchex-emu/socbot – restructuring branch](https://github.com/marchex-emu/socbot/tree/restructuring/SocTool)

**Author:** Ken Boller  
**Last Updated:** April 4th, 2025 
**Audience:** SOC Engineering, DevOps, Security  

This document provides a full overview of the SOC Access Management project — including file structure, systems integrated, scripts updated/created, and how to test or run the project in production. It also outlines what's been completed, what remains, and how to maintain/extend the toolset during the author’s leave.

---

## 🧭 Project Overview

The **SOC Access Management Toolkit** allows the Service Operations Center (SOC) to manage user access across 20+ internal systems using a unified process:

- ✅ **CLI Tool** (access_management.py)
- ✅ **GUI Wrapper** (soctool.py)
- ✅ **Modular per-system scripts** (located in Systems/UIs/ and Systems/DBs/)
- 🔄 **Credential access being tested on SOC Cloud Workstation**  
- ❗ **VPN access not required for DBs – access via SSH tunnel/jumphost preferred**

---

## 📁 Repository Structure

Path:  
https://github.com/marchex-emu/socbot/tree/restructuring/SocTool

### Folder Breakdown:

bash
SocTool/
├── access_management.py      # CLI entry point for checking, granting, removing access
├── soctool.py                # GUI wrapper that calls the CLI interactively
├── Systems/
│   ├── UIs/                  # System integration scripts (API-based or UI tools)
│   │   ├── aws.py
│   │   ├── jira.py
│   │   ├── grafana.py
│   │   ├── adtrack.py
│   │   ├── ...
│   └── DBs/                  # DB-integrated systems (Oracle, Snowflake, etc.)
│       ├── nimui.py
│       ├── snowflake.py
│       └── ...
├── Utils/
│   └── rt_api.py             # RT ticket comment / integration helper
├── Logs/
│   └── access_management.log # Auto-generated log of actions and outputs
└── README.md                 # (Planned) Project overview and onboarding guide


---

- ❌ Secrets directory and the use of Python scripts with sensitive info such as secrets.py and config.py

python soctool.py

The GUI wraps the CLI, handling input validation and passing the --mock flag automatically as needed.

# 🧰 Credentials & Authentication 
## 🔐 SOC Workstation Strategy: 
Use the SOC Cloud Workstation VM at:
 - Centralized secure credential access via environment + local secrets
 - Wrapper in get_secrets.py being integrated for standardized access

## April Update:

 - LDAP auth confirmed working from the SOC VM using user’s credentials
 - OpenVPN connection failed repeatedly due to cloud-identity restrictions
 - IT confirmed VPN not necessary for VM — secure access is likely routed through an internal **jumphost**
 - SSH local port-forwarding is the recommended strategy for DB access

as the secure host for: 
- LDAP credentials 
- API tokens (Grafana, JIRA, Auth0, PagerDuty, etc.) 
- DB passwords (Oracle, Snowflake) 

> Credentials are retrieved securely via the secret.get_secret("KEY_NAME") interface, which wraps local environment or file-based storage on the SOC Cloud Workstation.

- RT ticket integration via rt_api.py supports adding comments or triggering escalations 
- Each script logs its own activity independently

*   🧠 Working theory: DB is only accessible from inside the protected subnet

    *   Current Adtrack DB host/port
        
    *   DB type (PostgreSQL vs. Oracle)
        
    *   Jumphost strategy for access

*   No secrets stored in repo
    
*   MOCK_MODE is default unless overridden
    
*   Real credentials stored **only** on SOC VM / Bitwarden
    
*   Least privilege principle followed in each script

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI)
----------------------------------------------------
✅ Provides a GUI wrapper for access_management.py.
✅ Enforces LDAP authentication before executing actions.
✅ Calls access_management.py for check, grant, and remove actions.
✅ Mock mode enabled by default for safety.
✅ Optional RT Ticket logging.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, SIMPLE, AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "access_management.py")

# ✅ Ensure Logs directory exists
os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")

# ✅ Updated logging: file + console
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.DEBUG,
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler(LOG_FILE),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    ]
)

LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Function to execute access_management.py
def execute_access_action(action, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_mode, log_area):
    """Runs access_management.py in a subprocess and updates GUI logs."""

    def run():
        try:
            args = ["python3", ACCESS_SCRIPT, action, target_user, "--ldap_user", ldap_user, "--ldap_pass", ldap_pass]

            if rt_ticket:
                args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])
            if mock_mode:
                args.append("--mock")


            process = subprocess.Popen(
                args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1
            )

            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line.strip() + "\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line.strip()}\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n", "error")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {ACCESS_SCRIPT}: {str(e)}")

    thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
    thread.start()


# ✅ Function to create GUI window for actions
def open_access_window(action, show_mock_mode=True):
    """Creates a GUI window to handle access actions."""

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action.capitalize()} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action.capitalize()} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # ✅ LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Username:").pack()
    ldap_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Target LDAP Username:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ RT Ticket (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ Mock Mode (Enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # ✅ Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """Executes the access action when the button is clicked."""
        ldap_user = ldap_user_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "LDAP username, password, and target user are required.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} access script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        execute_access_action(action, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_mode.get(), log_area)

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


# ✅ Function to open RT queue clearing window
def open_clear_rt_window():
    """Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time."""

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script("clear_rt", [], log_area)


# ✅ GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("check", show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("grant", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("remove", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# ✅ Start GUI
root.mainloop()




"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
