#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import getpass
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core, SIMPLE
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIRS = [
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "UIs"),
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "DBs")
]  # Locate Systems/UIs and 'System/DBs' folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}")

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}")
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}")
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}")
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    found_any = False

    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        if not os.path.exists(directory):
            continue  # silently skip missing dirs

        found_any = True

        for script in os.listdir(directory):
            if script.endswith(".py"):
                system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
                script_path = os.path.join(directory, script)

                try:
                    cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "check", target_user]
                    process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True, encoding="utf-8", bufsize=1)
                    stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                    if stdout_output.strip():
                        print(f"✅ {system_name}: {stdout_output.strip()}")
                        access_list.append(system_name)

                    if stderr_output.strip():
                        print(f"⚠️ {system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")
                        logging.error(f"{system_name} Error: {stderr_output.strip()}")

                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}")
                    logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    if not found_any:
        print("❌ Error: No valid system directories found (expected Systems/UIs or Systems/DBs).")
        logging.error("No system directories found.")

    return access_list


def find_script(system_name):
    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        script_path = os.path.join(directory, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            return script_path
    return None


# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "remove", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")


# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "grant", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")


def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)




import json
import os
import logging

SECRETS_FILE = os.environ.get("SOC_SECRET_FILE", os.path.expanduser("~/soc-secrets/creds.json"))

def get_secret(key):
    """Retrieve secret from local JSON file."""
    try:
        with open(SECRETS_FILE, 'r') as f:
            secrets = json.load(f)
        return secrets.get(key)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Secrets file not found at {SECRETS_FILE}")
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        logging.error("❌ Secrets file is not valid JSON.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error loading secret '{key}': {e}")
    return None




# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "..", "..", "Utils"))

from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            # Example insert — customize based on your DB schema
            cur.execute("""
                INSERT INTO at_user (email, name, status, staff_level)
                VALUES (%s, %s, 'active', %s)
                ON CONFLICT (email) DO UPDATE SET status = 'active'
            """, (user_email, real_name, 'staff' if is_staff else 'user'))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant access to {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Grant failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# 🔐 Local Secrets Handling – SOC Tool

This tool uses a simple JSON-based local credential store located at:

To add a new secret:
1. SSH into the SOC workstation: youruser@soc1.az-eus-vws.marchex.com
2. Edit Secrets/secrets.json and add your new key-value pair.
3. That’s it. Scripts will auto-load from this file.

- File is ignored via .gitignore
- Used only from the SOC VM

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI)
----------------------------------------------------
✅ Provides a GUI wrapper for access_management.py.
✅ Enforces LDAP authentication before executing actions.
✅ Calls access_management.py for check, grant, and remove actions.
✅ Mock mode enabled by default for safety.
✅ Optional RT Ticket logging.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading
import logging
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, SIMPLE, AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  
LOGS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "access_management.py")

# ✅ Ensure Logs directory exists
os.makedirs(LOGS_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOGS_DIR, "soctool.log")

# ✅ Updated logging: file + console
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.DEBUG,
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler(LOG_FILE),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    ]
)

LDAP_SERVER = "ldaps://10.90.255.145"  # Update as needed

# ✅ Function to execute access_management.py
def execute_access_action(action, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_mode, log_area):
    """Runs access_management.py in a subprocess and updates GUI logs."""

    def run():
        try:
            args = ["python3", ACCESS_SCRIPT, action, target_user, "--ldap_user", ldap_user, "--ldap_pass", ldap_pass]

            if rt_ticket:
                args.extend(["--rt_ticket", rt_ticket])
            if mock_mode:
                args.append("--mock")


            process = subprocess.Popen(
                args,
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",
                bufsize=1
            )

            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line.strip() + "\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {line.strip()}\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {str(e)}\n", "error")
            logging.error(f"Error executing {ACCESS_SCRIPT}: {str(e)}")

    thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
    thread.start()


# ✅ Function to create GUI window for actions
def open_access_window(action, show_mock_mode=True):
    """Creates a GUI window to handle access actions."""

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action.capitalize()} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action.capitalize()} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # ✅ LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Username:").pack()
    ldap_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Your LDAP Password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Target LDAP Username:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ RT Ticket (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # ✅ Mock Mode (Enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # ✅ Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """Executes the access action when the button is clicked."""
        ldap_user = ldap_user_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() if rt_ticket_entry.get().strip() else None

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "LDAP username, password, and target user are required.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} access script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        execute_access_action(action, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_mode.get(), log_area)

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


# ✅ Function to open RT queue clearing window
def open_clear_rt_window():
    """Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time."""

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    execute_script("clear_rt", [], log_area)


# ✅ GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("check", show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("grant", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("remove", show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# ✅ Start GUI
root.mainloop()

SOC SOP uiAccessAFR
SOC SOP uiAccessJIRA | SOC SOP uiNimUI | SOC SOP uiAccessPagerDuty | SOC SOP uiRT | SOC SOP uiAccessAFR
Jump to navigationJump to search
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the AFR aka Advertiser Facing Reporting.

The URL for AFR is: https://onlinereports.com


Adding AccessRemoving Access

1. To grant access to AFR use these steps: [AFR Login Creation SOP]

Make sure to check out the general tab to know where to run the SQL command.

Removing Access

1. To remove access from AFR use these steps: [AFR Disable Account SOP]

Make sure to check out the general tab to know where to run the SQL command.






SOC SOP AFR
(Redirected from SOC SOP PROC AFR)

6	Remove CIDs from a Client Role Login

GeneralDisplay AFR Login InformationCreate a AFR User Role LoginCreate AFR Client Role LoginRemove AIDs from a User Role LoginRemove CIDs from a Client Role LoginCreate AFR Marchex Role LoginReset AFR user passwordUpdate AFR user nameRe-enable AFR loginDisable AFR login
Procedure Overview
The User role allows a login to access one or more Account IDs under a given CID. This procedure creates an AFR login with the User role. It also grants access to one or more AIDs that live under a specific CID. A given login can only access the Account IDs under one CID, so multiple logins will be needed if access to accounts across multiple CIDs are desired.


Procedure Name
usp_create_afr_user_login()


Input Parameters

username (Optional. We typically leave this null unless we have a specific reason not to.)
password (optional only if adding AIDs to an existing login)
email_address
CID
One or more comma-seaprated AIDs (For example: '6788' or '6788,6789,6790')
Name of the person creating the new login or the ticket the work is being performed under
Action name. This is not currently implemented in this SProc, so this value is always NULL.

Procedure Details
1. The procedure validates the required input parameters for blank values.
2. If a username is passed in, the procedure validates if a login with the specified username already exists. If so, an error is thrown.
3. If no login exists with the specified username, a new login will be created and the username will be assigned to it. In this case, a password is required.
4. If no username is specified, the procedure will find the first User role login that matches the specified email address and CID. It then adds the specified AIDs under that CID.
5. If no login exists for the email/CID combination, then a new AFR login will be created.
6. When adding AIDs to a login, duplicate AIDs will be ignored. If any of the specified AIDs are marked as 'DELETED' for an existing login, they will be re-added.


Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login('<username>', '<password>', '<email>', <cid>, '<aid(s)>', '<explanation>', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);

Examples
1. Creates a new login and assigns it the specified username. Grants permission to AID 6788 under CID 22.
2. The same as above, but grants permission to multiple AIDs under CID 22.
3. Creates a new login without assigning the new account a username. Grants permission to AID 6788 under CID 22.
4. The same as above, but grants permission to multiple AIDs under CID 22.

1. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login('user1', 'password1', 'user1@test.com', 22, '6788', 'RT#126746', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);
2. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login('user1', 'password1', 'user1@test.com', 22, '6788,6789,6790', 'RT#126746', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);
3. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login(null, 'password1', 'user1@test.com', 22, '6788', 'RT#126746', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);
4. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login(null, 'password1', 'user1@test.com', 22, '6788,6789,6790', 'RT#126746', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);

GeneralDisplay AFR Login InformationCreate a AFR User Role LoginCreate AFR Client Role LoginRemove AIDs from a User Role LoginRemove CIDs from a Client Role LoginCreate AFR Marchex Role LoginReset AFR user passwordUpdate AFR user nameRe-enable AFR loginDisable AFR login
This page contains information on the stored procedures used to manage AFR 1.0 users in the back-end. All of the following sprocs should be executed against the primary Page database: elpagedb-master.marchex.com

mysql -h elpagedb-master.marchex.com -u nocbot -p

User levels:

User: The most basic user account. Normally these are generated as part of the new account setup process but occasionally that process fails or an additional user is required.
Client: A user than can access all accounts (AIDs) within a given client account (CID). For example, a Client account with access to CID 27 can see all the accounts under that CID.
Marchex: A staff level user with access to all accounts regardless of CID. Should be created only for Marchex employees.

(source: http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/AFR_Sprocs)

Displays details for all of the logins associated with the specified email address.

Create AFR Client Role LoginRemove AIDs from a User Role LoginRemove CIDs from a Client Role LoginCreate AFR Marchex Role LoginReset AFR user passwordUpdate AFR user nameRe-enable AFR loginDisable AFR login
Procedure Name
usp_create_afr_client_login()


Procedure Overview
Creates a new AFR login with the Cient role. It also grants access to additional CIDs for existing logins with the Client role.


Input Parameters

username (Optional. We typically leave this null unless we have a specific reason not to.)
password (optional only if CIDs are being added to an existing login)
email address
One or more comma-separated CIDs. (For example: '91' or '91, 27, 32')
Name of the person creating the new login or the ticket the work is being performed under
Action name. This is not currently implemented in this SProc, so this value is always NULL.

Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_client_login('<username>', '<password>', '<email>', '<CID(s)>', '<explanation>', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);

Examples
1. Creates a new login, assigns it the specified username, and grants Client access to the specified CIDs.
2. Creates a new login without assigning the new account a username. If a login already exists with this e-mail address, CIDs will be added to that login.

1. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_client_login('user1', 'password1', 'user1@test.com', '22,27', 'brief explanation here', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);
2. CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_client_login(null, null, 'user1@test.com', '22', 'brief explanation here', null, @out1, @out2, @out3);

Procedure Overview
1. The procedure validates the required input parameters for blank values.
2. If a username is passed in, the procedure validates if a login with the specified username already exists. If so, an error is thrown.
3. If no login exists with the specified username, a new login will be created and the username will be assigned to it. In this case, a password is required.
4. If no username is specified, the procedure will find the first Client role login that matches the specified email address. It then adds the specified CIDs.
5. If no login exists for the specified email address, then a new login will be created.
6. When adding CIDs to a login, duplicate CIDs will be ignored. If any of the specified CIDs are marked as 'DELETED' for an existing login, they will be re-added.

Note: This procedure does not appear to be implemented correctly at this time.


Procedure Name
usp_disable_access_to_account


Procedure Overview
Disables User role access to one or more AIDs under a given CID.


Input Parameters

username or email address
CID
One ore more AIDs in a comma-separated list
The name of the person doing the work or the ticket the work was performed under
Action name. This is not implemented and must be NULL.

Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_account('<username or email address>', <CID>, '<list of account IDs>', '<RT# or reason for disabling>', ""'', @out1, @out2, @out3); ''

Examples CALL express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_account('test@marchex.com', 22, '6789,6790,5465', 'brief explanation here', "", @out1, @out2, @out3);


Procedure Details
1. The procedure validates input parameters for required parameters. username or email, cid, list of aid, reason for disabling 2. if an AFR USER level login is found with the passed in username and CID then specified accounts will be deactivated for that user login
3. if passed in username is an email address, accounts will be deactivated from all the USER level logins associated with that email address and CID

Remove CIDs from a Client Role LoginCreate AFR Marchex Role LoginReset AFR user passwordUpdate AFR user nameRe-enable AFR loginDisable AFR login
Procedure Name
usp_disable_access_to_cids()


Procedure Overview
Removes CIDs from AFR logins with the Client role.


Input Parameters

username or email address
One or more comma-separated CIDs. (For example: '91' or '91, 27, 32')
Name of the person removing the access or the ticket the work is being performed under

Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_cids('<username or email address', '<list of client ids>', 'RT# or reason for disabling', @out1, @out2, @out3);

Examples 1. Removes access to CIDs 27, 32 and 66 for the login with the username "username1".
2. Removes access to CIDs 27, 32 and 66 for the login with the email address of b@c.com.

1. CALL express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_cids('username1', '27,32,66', 'RT889', @out1, @out2, @out3); <br>
2. CALL express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_cids('b@c.com', '27,32,66', 'RT889', @out1, @out2, @out3);

Procedure Overview
1. The procedure validates the required input parameters for blank values.
2. If a Client-level login is found with the specified username, the specified CIDs will be deactivated for that login.
3. If the passed in username is an email address, CIDs will be deactivated from all the Client-level logins associated with that email address.

Create AFR Marchex Role LoginReset AFR user passwordUpdate AFR user nameRe-enable AFR loginDisable AFR login
Procedure Name
usp_create_afr_marchex_login()


Procedure Overview
Creates a new AFR login with the Marchex role. This is effectively an admin-level account.


Input Parameters

username (optional)
password
email address

Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_marchex_login('<username>', '<password>', '<email address>', @out1, @out2, @out3);

Examples 1. Creates a new login and assigns it the specified username.
2. Creates a new login without assigning the new account a username.

CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_marchex_login('marchex_user', 'password', 'test@marchex.com', @out1, @out2, @out3);</code>
CALL express_pages.usp_create_afr_marchex_login(null, 'password', 'test@marchex.com', @out1, @out2, @out3);</Code>
Procedure Details

1. The procedure validates the required input parameters for blank values.
2. If a username is passed, the procedure validates if an AFR login with specified username already exists. If so, an error is thrown.
3. If no username is specified, the procedure will check if any Marchex-level login exists for specified email address. If so, an error is thrown.
4. If no username is specified and a non-MARCHEX login exists for the email address, a new MARCHEX login will be created in addition to the non-MARCHEX login.
Do not use this method thinking that you can upgrade a login to MARCHEX level. You will end up with two separate accounts. 5. If no login exists, a new Marchex-level login will be created.

RT# or reason for enabling

Examples CALL express_pages.usp_enable_afr_login('test_marchex_user', 'RT33333', @out1, @out2, @out3);


Procedure Details 1. The procedure validates input parameters for blank values.
2. The login with specified username will be enabled
3. If the username passed in is an email address, all logins associated with the specified email address will be enabled

Disable AFR login
Disable AFR login


Procedure Name
usp_disable_afr_login()


Procedure Overview
Disables all AFR logins associated with the specified username/email address


Input Parameters
username or email address
reason for disabling or RT#

Usage

CALL express_pages.usp_disable_afr_login('<username or email address', '<RT# or reason for disabling>', @out1, @out2, @out3);



Examples

CALL express_pages.usp_disable_afr_login('test-username', 'brief explanation here', @out1, @out2, @out3);


Procedure Details
1. The procedure validates input parameters for blank values
2. If no login is found with the specified username or email address, an error is thrown.
3. If logins with the specified username are found, they will be disabled
4. If the username passed in is an email address, all logins associated with the specified email address will be disabled.

SOC SOP uiAuth0
SOC SOP uiAccessPagerDuty | SOC SOP uiRT | SOC SOP uiAccessAFR | SOC SOP AFR | SOC SOP uiAuth0
Jump to navigationJump to search


GeneralAdding AccessRemoving AccessObtaining Keys and Client SecretsSOC Access Token ScriptTenantsNon-SOC Tab
Some general knowledge that doesn't really fit into a specific tab but it's good to have


Auth0 is used for clients to connect to Marchex's UIs, APIs, and platforms using their own credentials.
In some cases such as marchex-one-ui, some other services will get to apply their tokens on their behalf.


SOC account credentials in BitWarden


There are three different kinds of access that may be asked for:
Enterprise Connections
Applications
Individual Users


There are logs available if people have a hard time logging on and want us to dig in:
Go here!
You can search by connection name like:
 connection: <Name Here> 
so if someone needs you to look for specific logs regarding a client to see why something might be failing, that's the easiest way to do it.



If you need to send any service-related email to Auth0, use the prod tenant

Creating Applications
An auth0 Application allows customer software to authenticate and interface with their Marchex stuff. These are also known as API users

NOTE: There are 3 tenants in Auth0: marchex, marchex-dev, marchex-qa and omni-dev. You can switch tenants in the top right pull-down above "create application". If the ticket doesn't specify which tenant, reply back asking for clarification and stall the ticket.
Go here
Click "Create Application"
Put the name as requested into the upper "Name" field
Select "Machine to Machine App" if nothing else is specified by the requestor
If "Machine to Machine", choose "V4 API"
Click "Create"
Fill out any specifics provided.
Send the Client ID and Client Secret via email to the person requesting the application. Don't paste them in the ticket.
You will need the Client ID again when associating the Application to an Account

Creating Auth0 Admin Users (for managing Auth0 tenants)
Ask how long they need the access for, which tenant(s), and what application they need access to, and get CC approval for the request
Go here
For each tenant:
Click the dropdown in the upper right corner where the avatar is
Select "Switch tenant"
Select the requested tenant
Click the dropdown in the upper right corner where the avatar is
Select "Invite an Admin"
Type in the person's email, and select the application they requested access to. If it's all applications, give them access to all applications.
Click Add. The rest is up to them and they need to accept the request from their email
User will then get an email (if they don't see below "Confirmation Emails"). They will be directed to login and create a new password with the invite.
Switch the tenant back to marchex for the convenience of the next person


Confirmation Emails


As of 6/18/19, Auth0 is not sending confirmation emails when a user is added to a new Admin group. Link must be manually copied (using "Pending" link) and emailed to the user requesting access.

Removing Applications
Go here
Click on the application you wish to delete
Click on Settings (if you aren't already there)
Scroll to the bottom where it says <font-color=red>DANGER ZONE
Click Delete Application



Removing Users

You will need to go through all tenants and check for users AND admin users

Go here
Click on User Management and then Click on Users
Click on the user you wish to remove
Click on the "Actions" dropdown and select "Delete"
Click on "Settings" in the left-hand menu
Click the "Tenant Members" tab
Click "Remove" on the user you wish to delete
Repeat all steps for each tenant
Now we need to check the admin users for each tenant

TenantsNon-SOC Tab
Info on Tenants and how to create them when asked for


Tenants are basically the environments within our Auth0 instance.
To change tenants:
select the drop down in the upper right where it says "marchex SO"
Click "Switch Tenant"
Select the one you want


The three tenants we use currently are:
Marchex (this is the prod account)
Marchex-qa (qa account)
Marchex-dev (dev account)
Omni-dev (app-solutions)
We really only care about access to the prod tenant. If someone wants access to qa or dev, grant it.


On occasion, someone will ask for a specific Tenant.
If they want a personal tenant, TBD
If they want a custom agreement, TBD


Non-SOC Tab

Useful tips for requesting Auth0 access from the SOC

All requests should go through RT
Specify what kind of access is needed: Is it an enterprise connection, a user connection, or application? Follow below for your request type.


Enterprise Connection
Connection Name (Can be any identifying name so we know what company the account belongs to)
What kind of connection? For example: SAML, Google Apps, etc.
TBD further. Every connection type has a specific set of needed information, this will get us started though.



ClientIDs/Client Secrets
If you need IDs or Secrets, please provide the following information in your request ticket:
The name of the client (IE ProMax, Ford Direct, etc)
DO say that you are specifically looking for the Client ID and Client Secret
Let us know why you need it. For security reasons, we can't provide credentials to anyone at any time.



User Account
Email address
What account(s) they should have access to
Keep an eye out for an email that will have user credentials



Application Account
Application Name
Keep an eye out for an email that will have Client ID and Client Secret

import logging
import cx_Oracle
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Database Credentials (Stored Securely)
DB_USER = get_secret("_AFR_DB_USER")
DB_PASS = get_secret("_AFR_DB_PASS")
DB_DSN = get_secret("_AFR_DB_DSN")  # Example: "hostname:port/service_name"

# ✅ Check if Oracle Client is Installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

# ✅ Function to Check AFR Access
def check_afr_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to AFR."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating AFR access check for {username}.")
        return [{"USERNAME": username, "STATUS": "Active"}] if username in ["mockuser", "testuser"] else None

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = "SELECT USERNAME, STATUS FROM AFR_USERS WHERE USERNAME = :username"
        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username})
        result = cursor.fetchall()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        return result

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to query AFR for {username}: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant AFR Access
def grant_afr_access(username, email, full_name, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to AFR."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = """
        INSERT INTO AFR_USERS (USERNAME, EMAIL, FULL_NAME, STATUS) 
        VALUES (:username, :email, :full_name, 'Active')
        """
        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username, "email": email, "full_name": full_name})
        connection.commit()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove AFR Access
def remove_afr_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from AFR."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AFR access for {username}.")
        return True

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = "UPDATE AFR_USERS SET STATUS = 'Disabled' WHERE USERNAME = :username"
        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username})
        connection.commit()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed AFR access for {username}.")
        return True

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_afr_access(action, username, email=None, full_name=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage AFR access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_afr_access(username, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has AFR access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have AFR access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not email or not full_name:
            print("❌ Email and Full Name are required to grant access.")
            return

        success = grant_afr_access(username, email, full_name, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_afr_access(username, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed AFR access for {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage AFR Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--email", help="Email address (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--full_name", help="Full name (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_afr_access(args.action, args.username, args.email, args.full_name, args.mock)

import logging
import cx_Oracle
import sys

from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging

    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Database Credentials (Stored Securely)
DB_USER = get_secret("_AFR_DB_USER")
DB_PASS = get_secret("_AFR_DB_PASS")

# ✅ Check if Oracle Client is Installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

# ✅ Function to Check AFR Access
def check_afr_access(email, mock_mode=False):
    """Displays AFR login info for the given email address."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking AFR access for {email}")
        return [{"EMAIL": email, "CID": 22, "AIDs": "6788,6789"}]

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        out1 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out2 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out3 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)

        cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_show_afr_login_for_email", [email, out1, out2, out3])
        connection.commit()

        logging.info(f"Access Info: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
        return {"out1": out1.getvalue(), "out2": out2.getvalue(), "out3": out3.getvalue()}

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check AFR login info for {email}: {e}")
        return None

def grant_afr_access(username, email, full_name, mock_mode=False):

        """

        connection.commit()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

import logging
import cx_Oracle
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Database Credentials (Stored Securely)
DB_USER = get_secret("_AFR_DB_USER")
DB_PASS = get_secret("_AFR_DB_PASS")
DB_DSN = get_secret("_AFR_DB_DSN")

# ✅ Check if Oracle Client is Installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

# ✅ Function to Check AFR Access
def check_afr_access(email, mock_mode=False):
    """Displays AFR login info for the given email address."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking AFR access for {email}")
        return [{"EMAIL": email, "CID": 22, "AIDs": "6788,6789"}]

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        out1 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out2 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out3 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)

        cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_show_afr_login_for_email", [email, out1, out2, out3])
        connection.commit()

        logging.info(f"Access Info: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
        return {"out1": out1.getvalue(), "out2": out2.getvalue(), "out3": out3.getvalue()}

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check AFR login info for {email}: {e}")
        return None
    
# ✅ Function to Grant AFR Access
def grant_afr_access(username, email, full_name, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to AFR."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        query = """
        INSERT INTO AFR_USERS (USERNAME, EMAIL, FULL_NAME, STATUS) 
        VALUES (:username, :email, :full_name, 'Active')
        """
        cursor.execute(query, {"username": username, "email": email, "full_name": full_name})
        connection.commit()

        cursor.close()
        connection.close()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove AFR Access
def remove_afr_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from AFR."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AFR access for {username_or_email}, CID: {cid}, AIDs: {aids}")
        return True

    try:
        with cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN) as conn:
            with conn.cursor() as cursor:
                out1, out2, out3 = cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str)
                cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_account",
                    [username_or_email, int(cid), aids, explanation, "", out1, out2, out3])
                logging.info(f"Remove result: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
                return True
    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_afr_access(action, username, password=None, email=None, cid=None, aids=None, explanation=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage AFR access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        if not email:
            print("❌ Email required to check access.")
            return
        if check_afr_access(email, mock_mode):
            print(f"✅ {username} has AFR access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have AFR access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not all([email, cid, aids, explanation, password]):
            print("❌ Required: --email, --cid, --aids, --explanation, --password")
            return

        if grant_afr_access(username, password, email, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode):

            print(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        if not all([cid, aids, explanation]):
            print("❌ Required: --cid, --aids, --explanation")
            return
        if remove_afr_access(username, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode):
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed AFR access for {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ CLI execution
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage AFR Access via SOP Procedures")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("username", help="Username or email for action")
    parser.add_argument("--email", help="Email (required for check/grant)")
    parser.add_argument("--password", help="Password (required for grant)")
    parser.add_argument("--cid", help="Client ID (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--aids", help="Comma-separated AIDs (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--explanation", help="RT# or reason (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_afr_access(
        args.action,
        args.username,
        password=args.password,
        email=args.email,
        cid=args.cid,
        aids=args.aids,
        explanation=args.explanation,
        mock_mode=args.mock
    )
import logging
import cx_Oracle
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Database Credentials (Stored Securely)
DB_USER = get_secret("_AFR_DB_USER")
DB_PASS = get_secret("_AFR_DB_PASS")
DB_DSN = get_secret("_AFR_DB_DSN")

# ✅ Check if Oracle Client is Installed
try:
    cx_Oracle.init_oracle_client(lib_dir="/path/to/oracle_client")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"Could not initialize Oracle client: {e}")
    exit(1)

# ✅ Function to Check AFR Access
def check_afr_access(email, mock_mode=False):
    """Displays AFR login info for the given email address."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Checking AFR access for {email}")
        return [{"EMAIL": email, "CID": 22, "AIDs": "6788,6789"}]

    try:
        connection = cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN)
        cursor = connection.cursor()

        out1 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out2 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)
        out3 = cursor.var(cx_Oracle.STRING)

        cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_show_afr_login_for_email", [email, out1, out2, out3])
        connection.commit()

        logging.info(f"Access Info: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
        return {"out1": out1.getvalue(), "out2": out2.getvalue(), "out3": out3.getvalue()}

    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check AFR login info for {email}: {e}")
        return None
    
# ✅ Function to Grant AFR Access
def grant_afr_access(username, password, email, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to AFR using the stored procedure."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant AFR access to {username}.")
        return True

    try:
        with cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN) as conn:
            with conn.cursor() as cursor:
                out1, out2, out3 = cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str)
                cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_create_afr_user_login", [
                    username, password, email, int(cid), aids, explanation, None,
                    out1, out2, out3
                ])
                logging.info(f"Grant result: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
                return True
    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access for {username}: {e}")
        return False


# ✅ Function to Remove AFR Access
def remove_afr_access(username_or_email, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove AFR access using the correct stored procedure."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AFR access for {username_or_email}, CID: {cid}, AIDs: {aids}")
        return True

    try:
        with cx_Oracle.connect(DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_DSN) as conn:
            with conn.cursor() as cursor:
                out1, out2, out3 = cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str), cursor.var(str)
                cursor.callproc("express_pages.usp_disable_access_to_account", [
                    username_or_email, int(cid), aids, explanation, None,
                    out1, out2, out3
                ])
                logging.info(f"Remove result: {out1.getvalue()}, {out2.getvalue()}, {out3.getvalue()}")
                return True
    except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username_or_email}: {e}")
        return False


# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_afr_access(action, username, password=None, email=None, cid=None, aids=None, explanation=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage AFR access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        if not email:
            print("❌ Email required to check access.")
            return
        if check_afr_access(email, mock_mode):
            print(f"✅ {username} has AFR access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have AFR access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not all([email, cid, aids, explanation, password]):
            print("❌ Required: --email, --cid, --aids, --explanation, --password")
            return

        if grant_afr_access(username, password, email, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode):

            print(f"✅ Successfully granted AFR access to {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant AFR access to {username}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        if not all([cid, aids, explanation]):
            print("❌ Required: --cid, --aids, --explanation")
            return
        if remove_afr_access(username, cid, aids, explanation, mock_mode):
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed AFR access for {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove AFR access for {username}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ CLI execution
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage AFR Access via SOP Procedures")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("username", help="Username or email for action")
    parser.add_argument("--email", help="Email (required for check/grant)")
    parser.add_argument("--password", help="Password (required for grant)")
    parser.add_argument("--cid", help="Client ID (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--aids", help="Comma-separated AIDs (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--explanation", help="RT# or reason (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_afr_access(
        args.action,
        args.username,
        password=args.password,
        email=args.email,
        cid=args.cid,
        aids=args.aids,
        explanation=args.explanation,
        mock_mode=args.mock
    )
no lets look at the auth0.py script and see if it maybe also needs to be changed based off the SOPs i shared for auth0




import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Auth0 API Configuration
AUTH0_DOMAIN = "marchex.auth0.com"
AUTH0_MANAGEMENT_API = f"https://{AUTH0_DOMAIN}/api/v2"
AUTH0_CLIENT_ID = get_secret("_AUTH0_CLIENT_ID")
AUTH0_CLIENT_SECRET = get_secret("_AUTH0_CLIENT_SECRET")
AUTH0_AUDIENCE = f"https://{AUTH0_DOMAIN}/api/v2/"
AUTH0_GRANT_TYPE = "client_credentials"

# ✅ Tenants
TENANTS = {
    "prod": "marchex",
    "qa": "marchex-qa",
    "dev": "marchex-dev",
    "omni-dev": "omni-dev"
}

# ✅ Function to Get Auth0 Access Token
def get_auth0_token(mock_mode=False):
    """Fetch an Auth0 management API token."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real token request.")
        return "mock_token"

    url = f"https://{AUTH0_DOMAIN}/oauth/token"
    payload = {
        "client_id": AUTH0_CLIENT_ID,
        "client_secret": AUTH0_CLIENT_SECRET,
        "audience": AUTH0_AUDIENCE,
        "grant_type": AUTH0_GRANT_TYPE
    }
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("access_token")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to get Auth0 token: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Check Auth0 Access
def check_auth0_access(username, tenant, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Auth0 in a specified tenant."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Auth0 access check for {username} in {tenant}.")
        return [{"user_id": "mock_user_id", "email": f"{username}@marchex.com"}]

    access_token = get_auth0_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return None

    url = f"{AUTH0_MANAGEMENT_API}/users?q=email:{username}&search_engine=v3"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json()  # Returns user data if found
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check Auth0 access: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant Auth0 Access
def grant_auth0_access(username, email, tenant, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Auth0."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Auth0 access to {username} in {tenant}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_auth0_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    url = f"{AUTH0_MANAGEMENT_API}/users"
    payload = {
        "email": email,
        "user_id": username,
        "connection": "Username-Password-Authentication"
    }
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Auth0 access to {username}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Auth0 access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Auth0 Access
def remove_auth0_access(username, tenant, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Auth0."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Auth0 access for {username} in {tenant}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_auth0_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    user_data = check_auth0_access(username, tenant, mock_mode)
    if not user_data:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} not found in Auth0.")
        return False

    user_id = user_data[0]["user_id"]
    url = f"{AUTH0_MANAGEMENT_API}/users/{user_id}"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.delete(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Auth0 access for {username}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Auth0 access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_auth0_access(action, username, email=None, tenant="prod", mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Auth0 access based on the action selected."""
    if tenant not in TENANTS:
        print("❌ Invalid tenant specified. Use 'prod', 'qa', 'dev', or 'omni-dev'.")
        return

    if action == "check":
        access = check_auth0_access(username, tenant, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has Auth0 access in {tenant}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Auth0 access in {tenant}.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not email:
            print("❌ Email is required to grant access.")
            return

        success = grant_auth0_access(username, email, tenant, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted Auth0 access to {username} in {tenant}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant Auth0 access to {username} in {tenant}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_auth0_access(username, tenant, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed Auth0 access for {username} in {tenant}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove Auth0 access for {username} in {tenant}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Auth0 Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--email", help="Email address (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--tenant", choices=["prod", "qa", "dev", "omni-dev"], default="prod", help="Auth0 tenant")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_auth0_access(args.action, args.username, args.email, args.tenant, args.mock)

User Access
1. Go the AWS and login https://console.aws.amazon.com/

2. Typing IAM in the search box

3. Click users at the left side

4. Searching the username(email) you want to create, if it’s not existing clicking “Add user” to create it.

5. Typing the username(email), in the access type choose “AWS Management Console access” then using autogenerated password and check “Users must create a new password at next sign-in” after all, go the “next Permissions“

Tips: you should find the name which we need copy from in the request ticket, if not you should send Email to his/her manager to ask.

Modifying Policies and arns
Sometimes you'll get a ticket like this one that infra used to do, but we'll do it now.
1. There's a lot of grey area here, sorry
2. Go here
3. If the ticket is like the above, and they show you the permissions they have and the permissions they need, follow the bullets in this step. Otherwise go to step 4.

Click "Users" on the left, search for the user you need, and click on their email address
Under "Policy Name", expand all policies
Search for the arn that they have, so you can find the policy that needs to be updated. In the above example, if you look in the policy "MarchexDSEngPolicy", you will be able to see the resource group.
Click on "Edit Policy", and move to step 5
4. If the ticket is asking to add an arn to a specific group, you should use the bullets in this step.

Click "Policies" on the left, Search for the policy you want, and click on it
Click on "Edit Policy" and move to step 5.
5. Click on the JSON tab
6. Find the sections that have other arns in the "Resource" block that match the desired arn

For example, if the desired arn is "arn:aws:elasticloadbalancing:*:111781987845:loadbalancer/app/ds-*", you'd put it in a block or blocks that has elasticloadbalancing as the Action, with similar Resources.

7. Click "Review Policy", and "Save Policy"

3. Click on the best match for what you're looking for. There is not a good way to tell you which one to click on in an SOP, so if you're unsure you should ask someone, or just use your best judgement.

4. Click "Add user to group", and add the user requesting access

Introduction
AWS Cross Account Access has been setup to allow users logged in to the Management Console of the Marchex Infrastructure account to switch roles within the console and manage other AWS accounts linked to the Marchex Consolidated Billing account.

The user must already have an account in the Marchex AWS account. See Setting_up_your_AWS_Account for more info.

The user must first login to the Infrastructure console

Login URL: https://infrastructure-aws.signin.aws.amazon.com


Once logged in click on one of the links below to switch accounts. Not all users are granted access to all accounts.

Linked Accounts

Command Line Interface
Initial Setup
The profile for the cross account access needs to be configured before the scripts can be run. Run the following commands to set the source profile and the role arn:

      $ aws configure --profile <profile> set source_profile default
      $ aws configure --profile <profile> set role_arn <role-arn> 
Preconfigured .aws/config file
A sample .aws/config file with all of the above STS rules configured can be found here



The profile for the cross account access needs to be configured before the scripts can be run. Run the following command to create an initial configuration, you can enter anything for the key pair (or leave blank) as the values don't matter at this point:



      $ aws configure --profile <profile>
Next configure the ARN value in the aws profile configuration. This is a custom value which you can find on this page:

      $ aws configure --profile <profile> set arn <role-arn> 

Get the STS Credentials and configure the profile
Run one of the following two scripts to get the STS Credentials and configure the aws cli profile:

Perl Script
The perl script can be found here: set_sts_credentials.pl


      $ pod2text set_sts_credentials.pl
Bash Script
The bash script can be found here: set_sts_credentials.sh

      $ set_sts_credentials.sh -h

Use and Enjoy
You can now use the aws cli with the '--profile' option for any cli command

      $ aws --profile <profile> s3 ls
      $ aws --profile <profile> ec2 describe-instances

heres my current aws.py script




"""
AWS IAM Access Management Script
---------------------------------------------------
✅ Check, Grant, and Remove AWS IAM access.
✅ Integrates with SOC Access Management Tool.
✅ Supports Mock Mode for safe testing.
"""

import logging
import subprocess
import shutil
import json
import argparse
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Function to check if AWS CLI is installed
def check_aws_cli():
    """Check if AWS CLI is installed."""
    if not shutil.which("aws"):
        logging.error("❌ AWS CLI is not installed. Please install it using 'pip install awscli'.")
        return False
    return True

# ✅ Function to retrieve AWS IAM users
def get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Retrieve the list of AWS IAM users."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Simulating AWS IAM user list retrieval.")
        return {"mockuser1", "mockuser2", "mockadmin"}  # Simulated AWS users

    try:
        output = subprocess.check_output(
            ['aws', 'iam', 'list-users', '--profile', auth_user],
            stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
        )
        users = json.loads(output).get('Users', [])
        return {user['UserName'] for user in users}
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ AWS CLI error: {e.output.decode().strip()}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to check if a user has AWS IAM access
def check_access(user, auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Check if the user has AWS IAM access."""
    if not check_aws_cli():
        return None

    aws_users = get_aws_users(auth_user, mock_mode)
    if aws_users is None:
        return None

    if user in aws_users:
        logging.info(f"✅ {user} has AWS IAM access.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {user} does NOT have AWS IAM access.")
        return False

# ✅ Function to grant AWS IAM access
def grant_access(user, auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Grant AWS IAM access to a user."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would create AWS IAM user {user}.")
        return

    try:
        subprocess.check_output(
            ['aws', 'iam', 'create-user', '--profile', auth_user, '--user-name', user],
            stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
        )
        logging.info(f"✅ AWS IAM user {user} created successfully.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to create AWS IAM user {user}: {e.output.decode().strip()}")

# ✅ Function to remove AWS IAM access
def remove_access(user, auth_user, mock_mode):
    """Remove AWS IAM access for a given user."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove AWS IAM access for {user}.")
        return

    try:
        subprocess.check_output(
            ['aws', 'iam', 'delete-user', '--profile', auth_user, '--user-name', user],
            stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
        )
        logging.info(f"✅ AWS IAM access removed for {user}.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove AWS IAM access for {user}: {e.output.decode().strip()}")

# ✅ Main function
def main():
    """Execute the AWS IAM Access Management script based on user action."""

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="AWS IAM Access Management Script")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform (check, grant, remove)")
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Username to manage AWS IAM access")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")
    parser.add_argument("--auth_user", default="default", help="AWS profile to use for authentication (default profile used if not specified)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    if args.action == "check":
        result = check_access(args.target_user, args.auth_user, args.mock)
        print(f"🔹 AWS IAM Check Result: {'✅ Has Access' if result else '❌ No Access'}")
    
    elif args.action == "grant":
        grant_access(args.target_user, args.auth_user, args.mock)
        print(f"✅ Granted AWS IAM access to {args.target_user}.")

    elif args.action == "remove":
        remove_access(args.target_user, args.auth_user, args.mock)
        print(f"✅ Removed AWS IAM access from {args.target_user}.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
