"""
AWS IAM Access Management Script
---------------------------------------------------
✅ Check, Grant, and Remove AWS IAM access.
✅ Integrates with SOC Access Management Tool.
✅ Supports Mock Mode for safe testing.
"""

import logging
import subprocess
import shutil
import json
import argparse
import sys
import os

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Function to check if AWS CLI is installed
def check_aws_cli():
    """Check if AWS CLI is installed."""
    if not shutil.which("aws"):
        logging.error("❌ AWS CLI is not installed. Please install it using 'pip install awscli'.")
        return False
    return True

# ✅ Run AWS CLI command
def aws_cmd(cmd_list, mock, mask_keys=False):
    if mock:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would run: {' '.join(cmd_list)}")
        return None

    try:
        output = subprocess.check_output(cmd_list, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
        result = json.loads(output.decode()) if output else {}
        if mask_keys and 'AccessKey' in result:
            result['AccessKey']['SecretAccessKey'] = '***'
        return result
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ AWS CLI error: {e.output.decode().strip()}")
        return None

# ✅ Check if user exists
def check_user_exists(username, profile, mock):
    result = aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'list-users', '--profile', profile], mock)
    if not result:
        return False
    return any(user['UserName'] == username for user in result.get("Users", []))

# ✅ Create AWS IAM User
def create_user(username, profile, mock):
    return aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'create-user', '--user-name', username, '--profile', profile], mock)

# ✅ Grant Console Access
def grant_console_access(username, password, profile, group=None, mock=False):
    logging.info(f"➡️ Granting console access to {username}")
    aws_cmd([
        'aws', 'iam', 'create-login-profile',
        '--user-name', username,
        '--password', password,
        '--password-reset-required',
        '--profile', profile
    ], mock)

    if group:
        aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'add-user-to-group', '--user-name', username,
                 '--group-name', group, '--profile', profile], mock)

# ✅ Grant Programmatic Access
def grant_programmatic_access(username, profile, mock=False):
    logging.info(f"➡️ Granting programmatic access to {username}")
    result = aws_cmd([
        'aws', 'iam', 'create-access-key',
        '--user-name', username,
        '--profile', profile
    ], mock, mask_keys=True)
    if result:
        logging.info(f"🔑 AccessKeyId: {result['AccessKey']['AccessKeyId']}")
        return result
    return None

# ✅ Copy Permissions from Existing User
def copy_user_permissions(source_user, target_user, profile, mock=False):
    result = aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'list-attached-user-policies',
                      '--user-name', source_user, '--profile', profile], mock)
    if not result:
        return
    for policy in result.get("AttachedPolicies", []):
        aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'attach-user-policy',
                 '--user-name', target_user,
                 '--policy-arn', policy['PolicyArn'],
                 '--profile', profile], mock)

# ✅ Remove AWS IAM User Access
def remove_user(username, profile, mock):
    logging.info(f"➡️ Removing user {username} and associated credentials")

    if mock:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would delete user: {username}")
        return

    # Remove login profile
    aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-login-profile',
             '--user-name', username, '--profile', profile], mock)

    # Delete access keys
    keys = aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'list-access-keys',
                    '--user-name', username, '--profile', profile], mock)
    for key in keys.get("AccessKeyMetadata", []):
        aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-access-key',
                 '--user-name', username,
                 '--access-key-id', key["AccessKeyId"],
                 '--profile', profile], mock)

    # Remove from groups
    groups = aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'list-groups-for-user',
                      '--user-name', username, '--profile', profile], mock)
    for group in groups.get("Groups", []):
        aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'remove-user-from-group',
                 '--user-name', username,
                 '--group-name', group["GroupName"],
                 '--profile', profile], mock)

    # Finally, delete user
    aws_cmd(['aws', 'iam', 'delete-user',
             '--user-name', username, '--profile', profile], mock)

# ✅ Main function
def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="AWS IAM Access Management Script")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("username", help="Username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--type", choices=["console", "programmatic", "billing"], help="Type of access to grant")
    parser.add_argument("--password", help="Password (required for console/billing user)")
    parser.add_argument("--group", help="IAM group to attach user to")
    parser.add_argument("--copy-from", help="Copy permissions from this user")
    parser.add_argument("--auth_user", default="default", help="AWS profile")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    if not check_aws_cli():
        return

    if args.action == "check":
        has_access = check_user_exists(args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock)
        print(f"🔹 AWS IAM Check Result: {'✅ Has Access' if has_access else '❌ No Access'}")

    elif args.action == "grant":
        if check_user_exists(args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock):
            logging.info(f"ℹ️ User {args.username} already exists.")
        else:
            create_user(args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock)

        if args.type in ["console", "billing"]:
            if not args.password:
                logging.error("❌ Password is required for console or billing users.")
                return
            group = args.group or ("Billing" if args.type == "billing" else None)
            grant_console_access(args.username, args.password, args.auth_user, group, args.mock)

        if args.type == "programmatic":
            grant_programmatic_access(args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock)

        if args.copy_from:
            copy_user_permissions(args.copy_from, args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock)

        print(f"✅ Granted AWS IAM access to {args.username}.")

    elif args.action == "remove":
        remove_user(args.username, args.auth_user, args.mock)
        print(f"✅ Removed AWS IAM access from {args.username}.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Description
This SOP is for adding and removing user access to various groups within portal.azure.com 

Note: The following steps allow you to easily add multiple users to a group, but in the case that you need to add one user to multiple groups, it may be faster directly from their account. Shortcut. 

== Adding Users ==

Go to portal.azure.com 
In the search bar at the top, look for Microsoft Entra ID.
Click "Groups" in the side panel. Shortcut. 
Use the search bar to look for the group name mentioned in the ticket.
Click "Members" in the side panel.
Click the "Add Members" button.
Search for the name of the user/s you need to add and click their checkbox.
Click "Select" at the bottom of the window to finalize your selections and add the users.
== Removing Users ==

Go to portal.azure.com 
In the search bar at the top, look for Microsoft Entra ID.
Click "Groups" in the side panel. Shortcut. 
Use the search bar to look for the group name mentioned in the ticket.
Click "Members" in the side panel.
Select the users you need to remove and click the "remove" button.

import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Azure API Configuration
AZURE_TENANT_ID = get_secret("_AZURE_TENANT_ID")
AZURE_CLIENT_ID = get_secret("_AZURE_CLIENT_ID")
AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET = get_secret("_AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET")
AZURE_GRAPH_API = "https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0"

# ✅ Function to Get Azure Access Token
def get_azure_token(mock_mode=False):
    """Fetch an Azure authentication token."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real token request.")
        return "mock_token"

    url = "https://login.microsoftonline.com/{}/oauth2/v2.0/token".format(AZURE_TENANT_ID)
    payload = {
        "client_id": AZURE_CLIENT_ID,
        "client_secret": AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET,
        "scope": "https://graph.microsoft.com/.default",
        "grant_type": "client_credentials"
    }
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, data=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("access_token")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to get Azure token: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Check Azure Access
def check_azure_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Azure Portal."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Azure access check for {username}.")
        return [{"id": "mock_user_id", "displayName": username}]

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return None

    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/users?$filter=startswith(userPrincipalName,'{username}')"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("value", [])  # Returns user data if found
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check Azure access: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant Azure Access
def grant_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to an Azure Group."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    user_data = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
    if not user_data:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} not found in Azure.")
        return False

    user_id = user_data[0]["id"]
    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/groups/{group_id}/members/$ref"
    payload = {"@odata.id": f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/directoryObjects/{user_id}"}
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Azure access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Azure Access
def remove_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from an Azure Group."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    user_data = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
    if not user_data:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} not found in Azure.")
        return False

    user_id = user_data[0]["id"]
    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/groups/{group_id}/members/{user_id}/$ref"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.delete(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Azure access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_azure_access(action, username, group_id=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Azure access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has Azure access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Azure access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not group_id:
            print("❌ Group ID is required to grant access.")
            return

        success = grant_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        if not group_id:
            print("❌ Group ID is required to remove access.")
            return

        success = remove_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Azure Portal Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--group_id", help="Azure Group ID (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_azure_access(args.action, args.username, args.group_id, args.mock)

import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Azure API Configuration
AZURE_TENANT_ID = get_secret("_AZURE_TENANT_ID")
AZURE_CLIENT_ID = get_secret("_AZURE_CLIENT_ID")
AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET = get_secret("_AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET")
AZURE_GRAPH_API = "https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0"
AZURE_GROUPS = get_secret("_AZURE_GROUPS")


def resolve_group_id(name_or_id):
    return AZURE_GROUPS.get(name_or_id, name_or_id)

# ✅ Function to Get Azure Access Token
def get_azure_token(mock_mode=False):
    """Fetch an Azure authentication token."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info("[MOCK] Skipping real token request.")
        return "mock_token"

    url = "https://login.microsoftonline.com/{}/oauth2/v2.0/token".format(AZURE_TENANT_ID)
    payload = {
        "client_id": AZURE_CLIENT_ID,
        "client_secret": AZURE_CLIENT_SECRET,
        "scope": "https://graph.microsoft.com/.default",
        "grant_type": "client_credentials"
    }
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, data=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("access_token")
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to get Azure token: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Check Azure Access
def check_azure_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Azure Portal."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Azure access check for {username}.")
        return [{"id": "mock_user_id", "displayName": username}]

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return None

    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/users?$filter=startswith(userPrincipalName,'{username}')"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("value", [])  # Returns user data if found
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check Azure access: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant Azure Access
def grant_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to an Azure Group."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    user_data = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
    if not user_data:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} not found in Azure.")
        return False

    user_id = user_data[0]["id"]
    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/groups/{group_id}/members/$ref"
    payload = {"@odata.id": f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/directoryObjects/{user_id}"}
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Azure access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Azure Access
def remove_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from an Azure Group."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True

    access_token = get_azure_token(mock_mode)
    if not access_token:
        return False

    user_data = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
    if not user_data:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} not found in Azure.")
        return False

    user_id = user_data[0]["id"]
    url = f"{AZURE_GRAPH_API}/groups/{group_id}/members/{user_id}/$ref"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}

    try:
        response = requests.delete(url, headers=headers)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Azure access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_azure_access(action, username, group_id=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Azure access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_azure_access(username, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has Azure access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Azure access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not group_id:
            print("❌ Group ID is required to grant access.")
            return

        success = grant_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant Azure access to {username} in group {group_id}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        if not group_id:
            print("❌ Group ID is required to remove access.")
            return

        success = remove_azure_access(username, group_id, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove Azure access for {username} in group {group_id}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Azure Portal Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--group_id", help="Azure Group ID (required for grant/remove)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_azure_access(args.action, args.username, args.group_id, args.mock)

AZURE_GRAPH_API = "https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0"
AZURE_GROUPS = get_secret("_AZURE_GROUPS")


def resolve_group_id(name_or_id):
    resolved = AZURE_GROUPS.get(name_or_id)
    if not resolved:
        logging.info(f"🔎 Using literal group ID: {name_or_id}")
        return name_or_id
    return resolved

SOC SOP uiCallScoring
SOC SOP uiGitHub | SOC SOP engageSpotlightAccess | SOC SOP uiAccessChef DataBag | SOC SOP uiAccessChef | SOC SOP uiCallScoring
Jump to navigationJump to search

Contents
1	Description
2	General
3	Adding Access
4	Removing Access
Description
GeneralAdding AccessRemoving Access
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the Call Scoring.

Call scoring is part of Marchex Institute: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/Marchex_Institute

Adding AccessRemoving Access

1. Log onto [Last3] .

2. Add the user to the call-scoring-login authorization group.

If they are in a group or need to be added to a group you can do that and they will automatically be added. Just sync the dynamic groups.
You might have to add them to static users if its needed.

Removing Access

1. Log onto [Last3] .

2. Remove the user to the call-scoring-login authorization group.

If they are in a group or need to be added to a group you can do that and they will automatically be added. Just sync the dynamic groups.
You might have to add them to static users if its needed.

next lets look at callscoring, above is the SOP i found and below is my current callscoring.py script


import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Call Scoring API Configuration
CALL_SCORING_API_URL = "https://api.callscoring.marchex.com"
API_KEY = get_secret("_CALL_SCORING_API_KEY")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

# ✅ Function to Check Call Scoring Access
def check_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Call Scoring access check for {username}.")
        return [{"id": "mock_user_id", "username": username, "role": "scoring-user"}]

    url = f"{CALL_SCORING_API_URL}/users?search={username}"

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("users", [])  # Returns user data if found
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check Call Scoring access: {e}")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant Call Scoring Access
def grant_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Call Scoring access to {username}.")
        return True

    url = f"{CALL_SCORING_API_URL}/users/add"
    payload = {"username": username, "group": "call-scoring-login"}
    
    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Call Scoring access to {username}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Call Scoring access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Call Scoring Access
def remove_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Call Scoring access for {username}.")
        return True

    url = f"{CALL_SCORING_API_URL}/users/remove"
    payload = {"username": username, "group": "call-scoring-login"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Call Scoring access for {username}.")
        return True
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Call Scoring access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_call_scoring_access(action, username, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Call Scoring access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has Call Scoring access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Call Scoring access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted Call Scoring access to {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant Call Scoring access to {username}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed Call Scoring access for {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove Call Scoring access for {username}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Call Scoring Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

generate a new and improved complete version of my callscoring.py script that better adheres to my SOP

""" 
Call Scoring Access Management Script (via Last3/LDAP)
------------------------------------------------------
✅ Check, Grant, and Remove user access to Call Scoring via LDAP group membership.
✅ Follows SOC SOP for call-scoring-login group management.
✅ Supports mock mode for testing without changes.
""" 

import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
import subprocess

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Group name constant from SOP
CALL_SCORING_GROUP = "call-scoring-login"

# ✅ Function to Check Call Scoring Access
def check_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would check if {username} is in group {CALL_SCORING_GROUP}.")
        return True

    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            ["id", username],
            capture_output=True, text=True, check=True
        )
        return CALL_SCORING_GROUP in result.stdout
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Could not check access for {username}: {e.stderr.strip()}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant Call Scoring Access
def grant_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant access to {username} by adding to {CALL_SCORING_GROUP}.")
        return True

    try:
        subprocess.run(
            ["usermod", "-aG", CALL_SCORING_GROUP, username],
            check=True
        )
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully added {username} to {CALL_SCORING_GROUP}.")
        return True
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to add {username} to group: {e.stderr.strip()}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Call Scoring Access
def remove_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Call Scoring."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove {username} from group {CALL_SCORING_GROUP}.")
        return True

    try:
        subprocess.run(
            ["gpasswd", "-d", username, CALL_SCORING_GROUP],
            check=True
        )
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed {username} from {CALL_SCORING_GROUP}.")
        return True
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove {username} from group: {e.stderr.strip()}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_call_scoring_access(action, username, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Call Scoring access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        has_access = check_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"🔹 Access Check: {'✅ Has Access' if has_access else '❌ No Access'}")
    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"{'✅' if success else '❌'} Grant Access Result for {username}")
    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_call_scoring_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"{'✅' if success else '❌'} Remove Access Result for {username}")
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Call Scoring Access (via LDAP group)")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="Username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no changes made)")

    args = parser.parse_args()
    manage_call_scoring_access(args.action, args.username, args.mock)

import logging
import json
import subprocess
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Chef Configuration
CHEF_DATABAG_PATH = "/etc/chef/data_bags/users"  # Adjust if needed
CHEF_CMD = "/usr/bin/knife"  # Path to knife CLI
CHEF_ORG = "marchex"  # Organization name

# ✅ Function to Check Chef Access
def check_chef_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Chef DataBag."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Chef access check for {username}.")
        return f"User {username} exists in DataBag (Mock Mode)"

    user_databag = os.path.join(CHEF_DATABAG_PATH, f"{username}.json")
    
    if os.path.exists(user_databag):
        with open(user_databag, "r") as file:
            user_data = json.load(file)
        logging.info(f"✅ {username} has Chef DataBag access.")
        return user_data
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Chef DataBag access.")
        return None

# ✅ Function to Grant Chef Access
def grant_chef_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Chef DataBag."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Chef DataBag access to {username}.")
        return True

    user_databag = os.path.join(CHEF_DATABAG_PATH, f"{username}.json")

    user_data = {
        "id": username,
        "groups": ["default"],
        "environment": "production",
        "permissions": ["read", "execute"]
    }

    try:
        with open(user_databag, "w") as file:
            json.dump(user_data, file, indent=4)
        
        subprocess.run([CHEF_CMD, "data_bag", "from_file", "users", user_databag], check=True)
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Chef DataBag access to {username}.")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Chef access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Chef Access
def remove_chef_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Chef DataBag."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Chef DataBag access for {username}.")
        return True

    try:
        subprocess.run([CHEF_CMD, "data_bag", "delete", "users", username, "-y"], check=True)
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Chef DataBag access for {username}.")
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Chef access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_chef_access(action, username, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Chef access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_chef_access(username, mock_mode)
        if access:
            print(f"✅ {username} has Chef DataBag access.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Chef DataBag access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_chef_access(username, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully granted Chef DataBag access to {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to grant Chef DataBag access to {username}.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_chef_access(username, mock_mode)
        if success:
            print(f"✅ Successfully removed Chef DataBag access for {username}.")
        else:
            print(f"❌ Failed to remove Chef DataBag access for {username}.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Chef Access")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_chef_access(args.action, args.username, args.mock)




import logging
import json
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ GitHub Repository Configuration
GITHUB_REPO = "marchex-chef-emu/databag_user_access_control"
GITHUB_API_URL = f"https://api.github.com/repos/{GITHUB_REPO}"
GITHUB_ACCESS_TOKEN = get_secret("_GITHUB_TOKEN")  # Store in Azure Key Vault or environment

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"token {GITHUB_ACCESS_TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.github.v3+json"
}

# ✅ Function to Check Chef DataBag Access
def check_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Chef DataBag on GitHub."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Chef DataBag access check for {username}.")
        return True  # Simulated access

    file_url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/contents/items/{username}.json"

    response = requests.get(file_url, headers=HEADERS)

    if response.status_code == 200:
        logging.info(f"✅ {username} has access in Chef DataBag.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have access in Chef DataBag.")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant Chef DataBag Access
def grant_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Chef DataBag by creating a JSON file in GitHub."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Chef DataBag access to {username}.")
        return True

    file_path = f"items/{username}.json"
    commit_message = f"Grant Chef DataBag access to {username}"
    file_content = json.dumps({"id": username}, indent=4)

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/contents/{file_path}"
    
    data = {
        "message": commit_message,
        "content": file_content.encode("utf-8").decode("latin1"),
        "branch": "main"
    }

    response = requests.put(url, headers=HEADERS, json=data)

    if response.status_code == 201:
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Chef DataBag access to {username}.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Chef DataBag access to {username}: {response.text}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Chef DataBag Access
def remove_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Chef DataBag by deleting their JSON file."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Chef DataBag access for {username}.")
        return True

    file_path = f"items/{username}.json"
    commit_message = f"Remove Chef DataBag access for {username}"

    # Get file SHA first
    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/contents/{file_path}"
    response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)

    if response.status_code == 200:
        file_sha = response.json().get("sha")
        delete_data = {
            "message": commit_message,
            "sha": file_sha,
            "branch": "main"
        }

        response = requests.delete(url, headers=HEADERS, json=delete_data)

        if response.status_code == 200:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Chef DataBag access for {username}.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Chef DataBag access for {username}: {response.text}")
            return False
    else:
        logging.error(f"❌ User {username} does NOT exist in Chef DataBag.")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_chefdatabag_access(action, username, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Chef DataBag access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ {username} has Chef DataBag access." if access else f"❌ {username} does NOT have Chef DataBag access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully granted Chef DataBag access to {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to grant access.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully removed Chef DataBag access for {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to remove access.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Chef DataBag Access via GitHub")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_chefdatabag_access(args.action, args.username, args.mock)

import logging
import requests
import base64
import json
import sys
import os

sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ GitHub Configuration
REPO = "marchex-chef-emu/databag_user_access_control"
API_BASE = f"https://api.github.com/repos/{REPO}"
TOKEN = get_secret("_GITHUB_TOKEN")
HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"token {TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.github.v3+json"
}
BRANCH = "main"

# ✅ Helper: Build GitHub file path
def build_file_path(username):
    return f"items/{username}.json"

# ✅ Check Access
def check_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would check if {username}.json exists in GitHub repo.")
        return True

    url = f"{API_BASE}/contents/{build_file_path(username)}"
    response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        logging.info(f"✅ {username}.json found in DataBag repo.")
        return True
    elif response.status_code == 404:
        logging.info(f"❌ {username}.json not found in DataBag repo.")
        return False
    else:
        logging.error(f"Error checking access: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant Chef DataBag Access
def grant_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would create {username}.json in GitHub.")
        return True

    file_path = build_file_path(username)
    payload = {
        "id": username
    }
    content = json.dumps(payload, indent=4)
    encoded = base64.b64encode(content.encode("utf-8")).decode("utf-8")

    url = f"{API_BASE}/contents/{file_path}"
    data = {
        "message": f"Grant Chef DataBag access to {username}",
        "content": encoded,
        "branch": BRANCH
    }

    response = requests.put(url, headers=HEADERS, json=data)

    if response.status_code == 201:
        logging.info(f"✅ Created {file_path} for {username}.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to create {file_path}: {response.text}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Chef DataBag Access
def remove_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would delete {username}.json from GitHub.")
        return True

    file_path = build_file_path(username)
    url = f"{API_BASE}/contents/{file_path}"
    get_resp = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)

    if get_resp.status_code != 200:
        logging.error(f"❌ File {file_path} not found or could not retrieve SHA.")
        return False

    sha = get_resp.json()["sha"]
    data = {
        "message": f"Remove Chef DataBag access for {username}",
        "sha": sha,
        "branch": BRANCH
    }

    delete_resp = requests.delete(url, headers=HEADERS, json=data)
    if delete_resp.status_code == 200:
        logging.info(f"✅ Removed {file_path} for {username}.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to delete {file_path}: {delete_resp.text}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_chefdatabag_access(action, username, mock_mode=False):
    if action == "check":
        exists = check_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ {username} has access." if exists else f"❌ {username} does NOT have access.")
    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to grant access.")
    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_chefdatabag_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Removed access for {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to remove access.")
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ CLI
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Chef DataBag Access via GitHub API")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("username", help="Username to manage in Chef DataBag")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()
    manage_chefdatabag_access(args.action, args.username, args.mock)

SOC SOP engageSpotlightAccess 
Cross Account Access | MIND+ Development Team Account | SOC SOP uiSalesEdge | SOC SOP uiGitHub | SOC SOP engageSpotlightAccess
Jump to navigationJump to search
Quick Note for Login Error for LDAP users

It is possible LDAP passwords to go out of sync and in that case we need to ask helpdesk to re-sync the LDAP credentials for UI.
If the user is logged in and sees a message about ad|Marchex|ldapusername not found, this usually means the user isn't added in the Marchex company in the UI, and it could happen because a change of name isn't reflected in the UI. We can use the process below to check and add the user to the list.

Quick Note to understand what this is
Go UI / One UI / Engage / Spotlight are all the same website (app.marchex.io) which uses login.marchex.io for logging in. login.marchex.io is a proxy for doing authentication with Auth0. login.marchex.io is also used for authentication for Speech 1.5 and Reporting

Creating Marchex Users for https://app.marchex.io , https://qa-oneui.marchex.com/ , and https://reporting.marchex.io

This website has had many names over the years. As of October 12, 2021 it is called Engage UI. Previous names include: One UI, Go UI, Edge UI, Sales Edge UI.

Marchex Users log into this UI with their LDAP credentials. They should use their username, not their full email address.

Contractor's and Vendor's email addresses usually have a -c or -v (e.g. username-c@marchex.com) but their LDAP username is usually just 'username'


FOR PRODUCTION: You can use the https://app.marchex.io UI to create the user in production.

FOR QA ACCESS: You can use the https://qa-oneui.marchex.com/ UI to create the user in QA.


App.marchex.io-initial-screen.jpg

Navigate to People -> Users on the left hand navigation panel.

App.marchex.io-user-list.jpg

With the search Icon search for the user to make sure they haven't already been added.

If they have not been added, click the 'CREATE NEW USER' button

Fill in the email, first, last names. If the user is a contractor or vendor fill in the ldapUsername field with the appropriate username. This field should not be required, but if it is fill it in with the username. Ignore the text below the form; it does not apply to LDAP users.

App.marchex.io-user-details.jpg

Choose Marchex as the Org Unit (this is a type-ahead search box). Choose MARCHEX_STAFF as the role.

App.marchex.io-org-role-details.jpg

After you have created the newly added user can you either send them an email or add them to the CC line of the ticket and then put this into the ticket:

To login:
1. Go to app.marchex.io
2. Put your username (the part before the @marchex.com. For example I would use "aderrick" and not "aderrick@marchex.com") in the username/alias
3. Put your Marchex LDAP password for the password
4. Enjoy your new access!




and heres my current engage.py script


import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Engage API Configuration
ENGAGE_API_URL = "https://app.marchex.io/api"
ENGAGE_API_TOKEN = get_secret("_ENGAGE_API_KEY")  # Store in Azure Key Vault or environment

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {ENGAGE_API_TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

# ✅ Function to Check Engage Access
def check_engage_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to Engage (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating Engage access check for {username}.")
        return True  # Simulated access

    search_url = f"{ENGAGE_API_URL}/users?search={username}"
    
    try:
        response = requests.get(search_url, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()
        users = response.json().get("users", [])

        if users:
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} has Engage access.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT have Engage access.")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check Engage access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant Engage Access
def grant_engage_access(username, email, first_name, last_name, mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to Engage by creating a new user."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant Engage access to {username}.")
        return True

    user_data = {
        "email": email,
        "first_name": first_name,
        "last_name": last_name,
        "username": username,
        "org_unit": "Marchex",
        "role": "MARCHEX_STAFF"
    }

    create_url = f"{ENGAGE_API_URL}/users"

    try:
        response = requests.post(create_url, headers=HEADERS, json=user_data)
        response.raise_for_status()

        if response.status_code == 201:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully granted Engage access to {username}.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response while granting Engage access to {username}: {response.status_code}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant Engage access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove Engage Access
def remove_engage_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from Engage."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove Engage access for {username}.")
        return True

    search_url = f"{ENGAGE_API_URL}/users?search={username}"
    
    try:
        response = requests.get(search_url, headers=HEADERS)
        response.raise_for_status()
        users = response.json().get("users", [])

        if not users:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT exist in Engage.")
            return False

        user_id = users[0]["id"]
        delete_url = f"{ENGAGE_API_URL}/users/{user_id}"

        delete_response = requests.delete(delete_url, headers=HEADERS)

        if delete_response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed Engage access for {username}.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Failed to remove Engage access for {username}: {delete_response.status_code}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove Engage access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_engage_access(action, username, email=None, first_name=None, last_name=None, mock_mode=False):
    """Manage Engage access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_engage_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ {username} has Engage access." if access else f"❌ {username} does NOT have Engage access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        if not email or not first_name or not last_name:
            print("❌ Missing required information for granting access. Provide email, first name, and last name.")
            return
        success = grant_engage_access(username, email, first_name, last_name, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully granted Engage access to {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to grant access.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_engage_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully removed Engage access for {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to remove access.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage Engage Access via API")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--email", help="Email address of the user (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--first_name", help="First name of the user (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--last_name", help="Last name of the user (required for granting access)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_engage_access(args.action, args.username, args.email, args.first_name, args.last_name, args.mock)

Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the GitHub.

Here is URL to access github: https://github.marchex.com/marchex-chef/

Here is URL to access New github https://github.com/marchex-chef-emu

Here is the URL to access LAST3: https://last3.marchex.com/last3/dashboard

Adding AccessAdmin Access to a RepoGranting Write Access to a RepoModifying Org AccessMoving a RepoArchiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes
These are the steps on how to grant access from GitHub.

Note:

Both FTEs and Vendors need appropriate manager approval (New Hire tickets are implied approval).

1. Go to Last3 and see if the user is already in the "dev" security group.

If they are a vendor (non @marchex.com email address), they likely will not be


2.

If they are already in dev, they already should have access. Any write issues they may be experiencing is not access-related
If they are not in dev, and they are a vendor, go on to step 3


3. Add the user to the Last3 Authorization Group github-users. Remember to sync after the changes are made.




System or App User
1. Make sure to coordinate first with Tools to ensure this app user addition is a known task, and also to make sure there isn't additional work needed to have the access granted

2. Add the user to github-appusers last3 auth

Admin Access to a RepoGranting Write Access to a RepoModifying Org AccessMoving a RepoArchiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes

If you get a request ticket where someone is asking to be an admin to a repo, this is the correct tab
1. Log into github using socbot credentials (LDAP password is in bitwarden)

2. Go to the repo in question

3. Click the little Settings gear on the center-top-ish right below the "watch" icon.

4. Click "Collaborators and Teams" on the left

5. At the bottom of the page, you'll see a list of collaborators.

If there is already an active admin, pass the ticket to them to complete the request (See below caveat).
Caveat: If the current admin doesn't make sense as the admin (for example: they've moved teams, or they're otherwise unavailable on leave or something), continue to step 6.
If there is not an active admin, continue to step 6


6. Check if the person requesting admin access is already a collaborator. They will be clearly listed under "collaborators"

If they are not, add them first with the "Add Collaborator" field
If they are there, use the dropdown next to their name and select "admin"

Granting Write Access to a RepoModifying Org AccessMoving a RepoArchiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes

If you get a request ticket for someone asking to have write access to a particular repo, this is the tab you need
1. Log into github using socbot credentials (LDAP password is in bitwarden)

2. Go to the repo in question

3. Click the little Settings gear on the top-ish right.

4. Click "Collaborators and Teams" on the left

5. At the bottom of the page, you'll see a list of collaborators.

If the person who is requesting write access is not there, add them first with the "Add Collaborator" field
If they are there, use the dropdown next to their name and select "write"

Modifying Org AccessMoving a RepoArchiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes

if someone is asking to be added to the Marchex or Marchex-Chef org, this is the tab you need
1. Log in to github using the socbot LDAP account. Password is in bitwarden

2. For the Marchex org, go here. For marchex-chef, go [Here is URL to access github: here]

3. click on "People". For a sanity check, search for the user first. If they're there, tell them they're already a member and ask what issues they're seeing. If they're not there, continue to step 4.

4. Put the user's name into the field in line with the "Add Member" button. If their name doesn't show up, you'll need to follow the steps in the Access tab. Otherwise, click "add member"

Moving a RepoArchiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes

If you got a request that looks like this, then this is the correct tab

1. Log in to github using the socbot LDAP account. Password is in bitwarden

2. Go to the repo in question.

3.

If there is a settings button, click it, and continue to step 9.
If there is NOT a settings button, continue to step 4.


4. Click on the little rocket in the upper right-hand corner. This will take you to a site-admin page for the repo

5. Click on "Security"

6. Click on the "Security" tab to the left if you are not already there.

7. Click the big, red "Unlock" button under the "Privileged Access" banner.

8. Give the reason for unlocking, and unlock it. You can now go back to the repo and you should see a "Settings" cog now. Continue to step 9.

9. Scroll to the bottom where it says Danger Zone

10. Click "Transfer"

11. It will ask you to type in the repo name, and to provide a new owner

Give it the repo name exactly as it is
Provide the org name "marchex"


12. Don't add any teams

13. Give it a few minutes, return to the repo, and click the "Settings" button again

14. Make whoever requested this the admin for the repo so that they can add whoever they need.

Archiving a RepoRemoving AccessNotes

If you got a request that looks like this, then this is the correct tab

1. Log in to github using the socbot LDAP account. Password is in bitwarden

2. Go to the repo in question, and click "Settings"

3. Scroll to the bottom where it says Danger Zone

4. Click "Transfer"

5. It will ask you to type in the repo name, and to provide a new owner

Give it the repo name exactly as it is
Provide the new GitHub username or organization name: "archive"



NOTE: To move a project out of "archive" it is the same process, but instead of setting the GitHub username or organization name to "archive", set GitHub username or organization name to: "marchex".

Removing AccessNotes
These are the steps on how to remove access from GitHub.

1. Is the user a Full Time Marchex user or a vendor?

Check their email address, it should be simple.
If they have an @Marchex.com alias, go to step 2.
If they are a vendor and have a non-Marchex email go to step 3.

2. Marchex Employee (marchex.com email)

If the requester is a developer they should already be in the 'dev' security group in Last3.
If the requester is not a dev, remove the user from the Last3 authorization group: github-users


3. Vendor (not a marchex.com email)

If the vendor only needed github access but NO pulley access, remove the user to the Last3 authorization group: github-restricted
If the vendor needed github access and pulley access, remove the user to the Last3 authorization group: github-restricted, then follow directions in the [pulley] .

Notes


The owners of individual repositories under marchex-chef can grant you access as needed. Please contact them.





import logging
import requests
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ GitHub API Configuration
GITHUB_API_URL = "https://api.github.com"
GITHUB_ORG = "marchex-chef-emu"  # Change if needed
GITHUB_TOKEN = get_secret("_GITHUB_API_KEY")  # Store securely

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"token {GITHUB_TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.github.v3+json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

# ✅ Function to Check GitHub Access
def check_github_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Check if a user has access to GitHub (mocked when MOCK_MODE=True)."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating GitHub access check for {username}.")
        return True  # Simulated access

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/members/{username}"
    
    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)

        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} is a member of {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return True
        elif response.status_code == 404:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} is NOT a member of {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return False
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response while checking GitHub access: {response.status_code}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to check GitHub access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant GitHub Access
def grant_github_access(username, role="member", mock_mode=False):
    """Grant a user access to the GitHub organization."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would grant GitHub access to {username} with role {role}.")
        return True

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/invitations"
    user_data = {"invitee_id": username, "role": role}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, headers=HEADERS, json=user_data)

        if response.status_code == 201:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully invited {username} to {GITHUB_ORG} as {role}.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response while granting GitHub access: {response.status_code}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant GitHub access to {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Remove GitHub Access
def remove_github_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    """Remove a user's access from GitHub."""
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove GitHub access for {username}.")
        return True

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/members/{username}"
    
    try:
        response = requests.delete(url, headers=HEADERS)

        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed {username} from {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return True
        elif response.status_code == 404:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} does NOT exist in {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return False
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response while removing GitHub access: {response.status_code}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove GitHub access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Handle Access Management Actions
def manage_github_access(action, username, role="member", mock_mode=False):
    """Manage GitHub access based on the action selected."""
    if action == "check":
        access = check_github_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ {username} has GitHub access." if access else f"❌ {username} does NOT have GitHub access.")

    elif action == "grant":
        success = grant_github_access(username, role, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully granted GitHub access to {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to grant access.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_github_access(username, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Successfully removed GitHub access for {username}." if success else f"❌ Failed to remove access.")

    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

# ✅ Run if Executed Directly
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage GitHub Access via API")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"], help="Action to perform")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="GitHub username of the user")
    parser.add_argument("--role", default="member", choices=["member", "admin"], help="Role for granting access")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (for testing)")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    manage_github_access(args.action, args.username, args.role, args.mock)

GitHub Access Management Script for SOC
---------------------------------------

)

GITHUB_ORG = "marchex-chef-emu"
GITHUB_TOKEN = get_secret("_GITHUB_API_KEY")

    "Authorization": f"token {GITHUB_TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.github.v3+json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}
# ✅ Function to Check GitHub Access
def check_github_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would check GitHub access for {username}.")
        return True

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/members/{username}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS)
        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ {username} is a member of {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return True
        elif response.status_code == 404:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} is NOT a member of {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return False
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response: {response.status_code}")
            return False
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error checking access: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Function to Grant GitHub Access
def grant_github_access(email, role="direct_member", mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would invite {email} to GitHub org with role '{role}'.")
        return True

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/invitations"
    payload = {
        "email": email,
        "role": role
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        if response.status_code == 201:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully invited {email} to {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.error(f"❌ Failed to invite {email}: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")
            return False
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error during GitHub access grant: {e}")
        return False
    
# ✅ Function to Remove GitHub Access
def remove_github_access(username, mock_mode=False):
    if mock_mode:
        logging.info(f"[MOCK] Would remove GitHub access for {username}.")
        return True

    url = f"{GITHUB_API_URL}/orgs/{GITHUB_ORG}/members/{username}"
    try:
        response = requests.delete(url, headers=HEADERS)
        if response.status_code == 204:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully removed {username} from {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return True
        elif response.status_code == 404:
            logging.info(f"❌ {username} not found in {GITHUB_ORG}.")
            return False
        else:
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ Unexpected response: {response.status_code}")
            return False
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove GitHub access for {username}: {e}")
        return False

# ✅ Main logic
def manage_github_access(action, identifier, role="direct_member", mock_mode=False):
    if action == "check":
        result = check_github_access(identifier, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ {identifier} has GitHub access." if result else f"❌ {identifier} does NOT have GitHub access.")

    elif action == "remove":
        success = remove_github_access(identifier, mock_mode)
        print(f"✅ Removed access for {identifier}." if success else f"❌ Failed to remove access.")
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")

2	Manage Postgres Accounts
GeneralManage Postgres Accounts
Requirements
Appropriate Approvals, Postgres access.


Description
This is an SOP outlining the process that the SOC follows in order to create or remove user accounts on Marchex's postgres DBs. Access Granted through these commands is Read Only access. If the user requires WRITE access, get appropriate authorization and then pass the ticket to the DBA on-call.

For DBs <user> is always just the user alias, so "user" not "user@marchex.com". NOTE: for LDAP authenticating databases, this MUST match the user's LDAP exactly. If the user has a "-v" in their alias, you will need to put quotes around their alias in the query in order for the role to be created properly.

NOTE: If a database is not referenced in SOC documentation, consult the DBA team before attempting to grant access

NOTE: If you are seeing ERROR: cannot execute DROP (or CREATE) ROLE in a read-only transaction, that means you are working on a slave DB, you should switch to another DB ( this ONLY affects DB that are in AWS)


Automated steps for adding users, The tedious manual steps are not needed. Do not remove them though.

ssh soc2.sea1
sudo su - socbot 
cd  /site/socbot/scripts/
python grantDBAccess.py

When you run it, you'll be prompted to put in the username, a password for any dbs that aren't LDAP (this WILL show up as plain text so that you don't forget the password used when you send it to the user),
and then finally a list of databases to grant access to. The list of databases are hostclasses without the 'db'.

For example, llmicrositedb-master and llmicrositedb-slave will be under llmicrosite
Unsure of what dbs you need? Well when it prompts you for your list of dbs, just type "m" and it'll show you all the available options.

It will output when it has successfully created an account on which databases, it will also output if it fails to create an account on which databases.




AWS Stuff

Use this: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_DBRedShiftAWS


MCA Adtrack (vspool, vspoolint)

Hosts for Adtrack DB Use the same password for all of these, since they login in one place at vspoolint.sea1

PROD = vsdb1.aws-us-east-1-vpc1.marchex.com
QA = qa-vsdb1.aws-us-west-2-vpc4.marchex.com

Note: Users do not connect directly to the database servers, instead they use the following connection information:

Host: vspoolint.marchex.com
Port: 5432
Database: adtrack_ro



How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to use postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-adtrack/conf/pgpass psql -U postgres -d adtrack


2.Run the following commands to create the account.

CREATE ROLE <user alias> WITH PASSWORD '<password>' LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 3;
GRANT adtrack_ro TO <user>;
\q





ARC DB

Hosts for ARC DB

Decommissioned

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-arc/conf/pgpass psql -d arc


2. Create the user accounts by running the following commands:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT dcm_all_read,ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q

Fortknox DB

Hosts for Fortknox DB

The primary where these steps need to be run changes from time to time. Here are some (maybe all?) of the hosts to try:

fortknoxdb1.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com
fortknoxdb2.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com 
fortknoxdb3.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com


Users do not connect directly to the database servers, instead they use the following connection information:
Host: fortknoxpool.sad
Port: 5432
Database: warehouse_ro (read-only) or warehouse (read-write)

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-fortknox/conf/pgpass psql -d warehouse


2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> WITH PASSWORD '<password>' LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT "fk-read-only", "fk-sandbox-ro" TO <user>;
\q



Additional access levels - fortknox sandbox write access. (Requires approval from Chris K)
GRANT "fk-sandbox-rw" TO <user>;
\q

GRANT ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q



To revoke access:

check their account first:

\dg <user>


If the user membership is only app_publisher_portal_ro, then:
 DROP ROLE <user>
 \q


Otherwise
REVOKE app_publisher_portal_ro FROM <user>;
 
\q

so given this new information lets take another look at both the adtrack script and the creds.json file to see what needs to be changed or updated with this new information to be able to connect to adtrack and test the adtrack script and then well continue to move thru each systems UI and DB scripts one at a time and test them all the same way




# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


import logging
import psycopg2
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            # Example insert — customize based on your DB schema
            cur.execute("""
                INSERT INTO at_user (email, name, status, staff_level)
                VALUES (%s, %s, 'active', %s)
                ON CONFLICT (email) DO UPDATE SET status = 'active'
            """, (user_email, real_name, 'staff' if is_staff else 'user'))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant access to {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Grant failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

heres my get_secrets.py and creds.json files for your review




import json
import os
import logging

SECRETS_FILE = os.environ.get("SOC_SECRET_FILE", os.path.expanduser("~/soc-secrets/creds.json"))

def get_secret(key):
    """Retrieve secret from local JSON file."""
    try:
        with open(SECRETS_FILE, 'r') as f:
            secrets = json.load(f)
        return secrets.get(key)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        logging.error(f"❌ Secrets file not found at {SECRETS_FILE}")
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        logging.error("❌ Secrets file is not valid JSON.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error loading secret '{key}': {e}")
    return None
