ill paste my access_management.py script below for your review.




"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import getpass
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core, SIMPLE
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIRS = [
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "UIs"),
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "DBs")
]  # Locate Systems/UIs and 'System/DBs' folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}", flush=True)

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}", flush=True)
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}", flush=True)
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}", flush=True)
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}", flush=True)
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    found_any = False

    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        if not os.path.exists(directory):
            continue  # silently skip missing dirs

        found_any = True

        for script in os.listdir(directory):
            if script.endswith(".py"):
                system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
                script_path = os.path.join(directory, script)

                try:
                    cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "check", target_user]
                    process = subprocess.Popen(
                        cmd,
                        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                        stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                        text=True,
                        encoding="utf-8",
                        bufsize=1
                    )

                    stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                    # Combine and normalize output
                    combined_output = (stdout_output or "") + (stderr_output or "")

                    # Basic success/failure logic
                    if "❌" in combined_output or "not have access" in combined_output.lower():
                        print(f"❌ {system_name}: {target_user} does not have access.", flush=True)
                    elif "✅" in combined_output or "has access" in combined_output.lower():
                        print(f"✅ {system_name}: {target_user} has access.", flush=True)
                        access_list.append(system_name)
                    else:
                        print(f"⚠️ {system_name}: Unable to determine access for {target_user}.", flush=True)

                    # Still log raw output for debugging
                    if stderr_output.strip():
                        logging.error(f"{system_name} STDERR: {stderr_output.strip()}")

                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}", flush=True)
                    logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    if not found_any:
        print("❌ Error: No valid system directories found (expected Systems/UIs or Systems/DBs).")
        logging.error("No system directories found.")

    elif not access_list:
        print(f"❌ {target_user} has no access to any known systems.", flush=True)

    return access_list


def find_script(system_name):
    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        script_path = os.path.join(directory, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            return script_path
    return None


# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "remove", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")


# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "grant", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")


def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            if system_to_remove in access_list:
                remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove)
            else:
                print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant)

    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(args.target_user, system_to_grant, args.mock)
    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter system to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(args.target_user, system_to_remove, args.mock)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI Only)
---------------------------------------------------
✅ CLI-based access management for SOC.
✅ Secure LDAP authentication via Azure Key Vault.
✅ Interactive access management (Check → Remove/Grant).
✅ Independent from GUI (SOC Tool calls this script).
"""

#Example CLI Usage
#python access_management.py check kboller
#python access_management.py grant kboller --rt_ticket 12345
#python access_management.py remove kboller --mock

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import getpass
from datetime import datetime
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, NTLM, ALL, core, SIMPLE
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret


# ✅ Ensure UTF-8 encoding to prevent errors
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")
sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")

# ✅ Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
SYSTEMS_DIRS = [
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "UIs"),
    os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems", "DBs")
]  # Locate Systems/UIs and 'System/DBs' folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")  # Correct path to Logs/
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# ✅ Set up logging
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "access_management.log")
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")


# ✅ Attempt to import rt_api.py (for RT ticket updates)
try:
    sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils"))
    from rt_api import add_comment
except ModuleNotFoundError:
    def add_comment(ticket, comment):
        logging.warning(f"RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")
        print(f"⚠️ RT API not found. Skipping RT ticket update: {ticket}.")


def authenticate_ldap(username, password):
    ldap_server = "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"  # Using the OpenLDAP host Tim referenced
    user_dn = f"uid={username},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"

    print(f"🔐 Trying LDAP bind as DN: {user_dn} to {ldap_server}", flush=True)

    try:
        server = Server(ldap_server, port=636, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
        conn = Connection(
            server,
            user=user_dn,
            password=password,
            authentication=SIMPLE
        )

        if not conn.bind():
            print(f"❌ LDAP auth failed: {conn.result['description']}", flush=True)
            return False

        print(f"✅ Authenticated to LDAP as {user_dn}", flush=True)
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ LDAP auth exception: {e}", flush=True)
        return False


# ✅ Prompt for missing inputs
def prompt_if_missing(value, prompt_text):
    """Prompt user for input if a value is missing."""
    return value if value else input(prompt_text).strip()


# ✅ Check user access
def check_user_access(target_user):
    """Checks all systems where the user has access."""
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    print(f"🔹 Checking access for {target_user} at {timestamp}", flush=True)
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {target_user}")

    access_list = []

    found_any = False

    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        if not os.path.exists(directory):
            continue  # silently skip missing dirs

        found_any = True

        for script in os.listdir(directory):
            if script.endswith(".py"):
                system_name = script.replace(".py", "").capitalize()
                script_path = os.path.join(directory, script)

                try:
                    cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "check", target_user]
                    process = subprocess.Popen(
                        cmd,
                        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                        stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                        text=True,
                        encoding="utf-8",
                        bufsize=1
                    )

                    stdout_output, stderr_output = process.communicate()

                    # Combine and normalize output
                    combined_output = (stdout_output or "") + (stderr_output or "")

                    # Basic success/failure logic
                    if "❌" in combined_output or "not have access" in combined_output.lower():
                        print(f"❌ {system_name}: {target_user} does not have access.", flush=True)
                    elif "✅" in combined_output or "has access" in combined_output.lower():
                        print(f"✅ {system_name}: {target_user} has access.", flush=True)
                        access_list.append(system_name)
                    else:
                        print(f"⚠️ {system_name}: Unable to determine access for {target_user}.", flush=True)

                    # Still log raw output for debugging
                    if stderr_output.strip():
                        logging.error(f"{system_name} STDERR: {stderr_output.strip()}")

                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"❌ {system_name}: Error checking access - {e}", flush=True)
                    logging.error(f"Error checking access for {system_name}: {e}")

    if not found_any:
        print("❌ Error: No valid system directories found (expected Systems/UIs or Systems/DBs).")
        logging.error("No system directories found.")

    elif not access_list:
        print(f"❌ {target_user} has no access to any known systems.", flush=True)

    return access_list


def find_script(system_name):
    for directory in SYSTEMS_DIRS:
        script_path = os.path.join(directory, f"{system_name.lower()}.py")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            return script_path
    return None


# ✅ Remove access from a system
def remove_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "remove", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Remove script for {system_name} not found.")


# ✅ Grant access to a system
def grant_access(target_user, system_name, mock_mode):
    script_path = find_script(system_name)
    if script_path:
        cmd = [sys.executable, script_path, "grant", target_user]
        if mock_mode:
            cmd.append("--mock")
        subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"✅ Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
        logging.info(f"Granted access to {system_name} for {target_user}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Grant script for {system_name} not found.")
        logging.info(f"Removed access to {system_name} for {target_user}")


def interactive_access_management(mock_mode=False):
    """Runs the interactive access management process."""

    # ✅ Prompt for LDAP credentials interactively
    ldap_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter your LDAP username: ")
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # ✅ Authenticate LDAP before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(ldap_user, ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)


    # ✅ Get the target LDAP username
    target_user = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the LDAP username of the target user: ")

    # ✅ Check access first
    access_list = check_user_access(target_user)

    if access_list:
        print("\n🔹 The user currently has access to these systems:")
        for i, system in enumerate(access_list, start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {system}")

        # ✅ Ask if access should be removed
        remove_choice = input("\nWould you like to remove access from any of these systems? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
        if remove_choice == "yes":
            system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
            remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove, mock_mode)
        else:
            print("❌ Invalid selection. System not found in the access list.")

    # ✅ Ask if access should be granted
    grant_choice = input("\nWould you like to grant access to a new system? (yes/no): ").strip().lower()
    if grant_choice == "yes":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant, mock_mode)
    print("\n🔹 Access management completed.")

# ✅ CLI Argument Parsing
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Manage SOC user access with LDAP authentication.")
    parser.add_argument("action", choices=["check", "grant", "remove"])
    parser.add_argument("target_user", help="Target LDAP username to manage")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_user", required=True, help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("--ldap_pass", required=True, help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT ticket number (optional)")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode")
    parser.add_argument("--system", help="Specific system to modify access for")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Authenticate before proceeding
    if not authenticate_ldap(args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass):
        print("❌ LDAP Authentication Failed. Access Denied.")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Route the action
    if args.action == "check":
        check_user_access(args.target_user)
    elif args.action == "grant":
        system_to_grant = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to grant access to: ")
        grant_access(target_user, system_to_grant, mock_mode)

    elif args.action == "remove":
        system_to_remove = prompt_if_missing(None, "Enter the system name to remove access from: ")
        remove_access(target_user, system_to_remove, mock_mode)

# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


import logging
import psycopg2
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspoolint.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    if "@" not in user:
        user_email = f"{user}@marchex.com"
    else:
        user_email = user

    search_param = vendor_email or user_email

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, real_name, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            # Example insert — customize based on your DB schema
            cur.execute("""
                INSERT INTO at_user (email, name, status, staff_level)
                VALUES (%s, %s, 'active', %s)
                ON CONFLICT (email) DO UPDATE SET status = 'active'
            """, (user_email, real_name, 'staff' if is_staff else 'user'))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to grant access to {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Grant failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, real_name, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

    "host": "vspoolint.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")

    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    if "@" not in user:
        user_email = f"{user}@marchex.com"
    else:
        user_email = user

    search_param = vendor_email or user_email

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:

            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        logging.error("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        cur.execute("""
            INSERT INTO at_user (email, status)
            VALUES (%s, 'active')
        """, (user_email,))
        conn.commit()
    except psycopg2.errors.UniqueViolation:
        logging.warning(f"User {user_email} already exists in AdTrack. Skipping insert.")
        print(f"⚠️ User {user_email} already exists. No changes made.")

    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        grant_adtrack_access(user)
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, is_staff)
    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        logging.error("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        cur.execute("""
            INSERT INTO at_user (email, status)
            VALUES (%s, 'active')
        """, (user_email,))
        conn.commit()
    except psycopg2.errors.UniqueViolation:
        logging.warning(f"User {user_email} already exists in AdTrack. Skipping insert.")
        print(f"⚠️ User {user_email} already exists. No changes made.")

    finally:
        conn.close()
    print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
    logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, is_staff)

    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

SOC SOP uiAccessAdTrack
SOC SOP uiAccessAdTrack
Jump to navigationJump to search

Contents
1	Description
2	Adding Access
2.1	If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
2.1.1	NOTE
3	Removing Access
Description
This SOP is for adding and removing access for the Adtrack UI, aka Marchex.IO

Adding AccessRemoving Access

When an account needs to be added by request/ticket use the following steps.


If a user requests access to the Adtrack UI also called Marchex.io and need access to the tool. Most of our requests are for "staff level" access. See "Adtrack Account standards" link below

Adtrack Account standards 
If the user doesn't ask for "Staff level", email them asking them if they do and make sure to give them the URL for Adtrack Account standards to help them
http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_adtrackUIAccountStandards

1. Log into Adtrack

Service Account & Password found in Bitwarden

2. Click the Client List tab in the UI.

3. Unless specified in the ticket create their account in the following group:

Marchex Voice Services (nee Voicestar) (This has been the historic place to put accounts for Marchex users.)

Note:

Sometimes you will have to match an account with another account.
The easiest way to do that is to open a two tabs in your browser.
In the first one, search in "Client list" using the target email (user to copy)
Then follow the below steps and just match up all the permissions.
4. Click on the Account Name, it will drop down, and click Account Settings.

5. Click Users

6. Click "New user".

7. Fill in the user's information:

Real Name
Email
Password [Password Gen]
NOTE:

If the email account is already in use, the tool will not let you use it again. You either have to alter the email with a Capital letter or find the other account and update that one.

8. Click submit at the bottom.

9. Search for the users account once more to provision it.

10. Using either given credentials from another account (Not preferred method) or [staff level] provision the account and click "update" at the bottom.

There are three specific pieces that Require more than the users manager approval: Bulk create /update Campaigns & accounts, Billing Write , and Edit Staff Permissions . See above staff level link.

11. Email the credentials to the user.


NOTE
Adtrack staff tools exist Here and will soon (hopefully) have a staff search function, at which point the above instructions will be thankfully obsolete.

Removing Access

When an account needs to be removed either from a separation or SOX audit or team change use the following steps.


1. Log onto [AdtrackUI/Marchex.io]

Service Account & Password found in Keypass

2. Click on "Client List"

3. In the top right enter the email address of the user you wish to remove.

This will return account groups with the email addresses in the users.

4. For all account groups found, perform the following:

Click on the account, it will drop down. click Account Settings
Click Users
Search again in the top right corner for the user's email address
Click on the correct user
Click User Settings
Set the status to disabled
Click Update

2	Manage Postgres Accounts
GeneralManage Postgres Accounts
Requirements
Appropriate Approvals, Postgres access.


Description
This is an SOP outlining the process that the SOC follows in order to create or remove user accounts on Marchex's postgres DBs. Access Granted through these commands is Read Only access. If the user requires WRITE access, get appropriate authorization and then pass the ticket to the DBA on-call.

For DBs <user> is always just the user alias, so "user" not "user@marchex.com". NOTE: for LDAP authenticating databases, this MUST match the user's LDAP exactly. If the user has a "-v" in their alias, you will need to put quotes around their alias in the query in order for the role to be created properly.

NOTE: If a database is not referenced in SOC documentation, consult the DBA team before attempting to grant access

NOTE: If you are seeing ERROR: cannot execute DROP (or CREATE) ROLE in a read-only transaction, that means you are working on a slave DB, you should switch to another DB ( this ONLY affects DB that are in AWS)


Automated steps for adding users, The tedious manual steps are not needed. Do not remove them though.

ssh soc2.sea1
sudo su - socbot 
cd  /site/socbot/scripts/
python grantDBAccess.py

When you run it, you'll be prompted to put in the username, a password for any dbs that aren't LDAP (this WILL show up as plain text so that you don't forget the password used when you send it to the user),
and then finally a list of databases to grant access to. The list of databases are hostclasses without the 'db'.

For example, llmicrositedb-master and llmicrositedb-slave will be under llmicrosite
Unsure of what dbs you need? Well when it prompts you for your list of dbs, just type "m" and it'll show you all the available options.

It will output when it has successfully created an account on which databases, it will also output if it fails to create an account on which databases.




AWS Stuff

Use this: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_DBRedShiftAWS


MCA Adtrack (vspool, vspoolint)

Hosts for Adtrack DB Use the same password for all of these, since they login in one place at vspoolint.sea1

PROD = vsdb1.aws-us-east-1-vpc1.marchex.com
QA = qa-vsdb1.aws-us-west-2-vpc4.marchex.com

Note: Users do not connect directly to the database servers, instead they use the following connection information:

Host: vspoolint.marchex.com
Port: 5432
Database: adtrack_ro



How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to use postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-adtrack/conf/pgpass psql -U postgres -d adtrack


2.Run the following commands to create the account.

CREATE ROLE <user alias> WITH PASSWORD '<password>' LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 3;
GRANT adtrack_ro TO <user>;
\q





ARC DB

Hosts for ARC DB

Decommissioned

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-arc/conf/pgpass psql -d arc


2. Create the user accounts by running the following commands:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT dcm_all_read,ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q

Hosts for Audience DB Decommissioned

Call Analytics DB

Hosts for Call Analytics DB

QA Master: shs-stg-mc2-writer.db.marchex.io
Prod Master: shs-prd-mc2-writer.db.marchex.io

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to connect to the database:

psql -h  shs-prd-mc2-writer.db.marchex.io -d postgres -U postgres


2. Create the user accounts by running the following commands:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT call_analytics_ro,authzone_ro,workspace_ro,notification_ro,conversation_sharing_ro,ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q

Fortknox DB

Hosts for Fortknox DB

The primary where these steps need to be run changes from time to time. Here are some (maybe all?) of the hosts to try:

fortknoxdb1.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com
fortknoxdb2.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com 
fortknoxdb3.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.marchex.com


Users do not connect directly to the database servers, instead they use the following connection information:
Host: fortknoxpool.sad
Port: 5432
Database: warehouse_ro (read-only) or warehouse (read-write)

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-fortknox/conf/pgpass psql -d warehouse


2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> WITH PASSWORD '<password>' LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT "fk-read-only", "fk-sandbox-ro" TO <user>;
\q



Additional access levels - fortknox sandbox write access. (Requires approval from Chris K)
GRANT "fk-sandbox-rw" TO <user>;
\q

QA Master: qa-srccmpgnsetupdb.som1

This database uses LDAP for users, no password resets

How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-srccmpgnsetup/conf/pgpass psql -d campaign_setup

2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT ldap_auth, campaign_setup_ro, search_structure_ro TO <user>;
\q

2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;

\q



publisher portal

Hosts for publisher portal DB Decommissioned Database: publisher_portal_db
How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-tax/conf/pgpass psql -d publisher_portal_db

2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias> LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT app_publisher_portal_ro TO <user>;
GRANT ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q



To revoke access:

check their account first:

\dg <user>


If the user membership is only app_publisher_portal_ro, then:
 DROP ROLE <user>
 \q


Otherwise
REVOKE app_publisher_portal_ro FROM <user>;
 
\q

Decommissioned
How to grant access:
1. Run the following command to start postgres on the host:

sudo -u postgres PGPASSFILE=/site/pgsql-tax/conf/pgpass psql -d taxonomy_db

2. Create the user account by running this command:

CREATE ROLE <user alias>  LOGIN CONNECTION LIMIT 5;
GRANT taxonomy_ro TO <user>;
GRANT ldap_auth TO <user>;
\q



To revoke access:
1. First check the user access:

\dg <user>


If the user membership is only taxonomy_ro, then:
DROP ROLE <user>;

\q
Otherwise:
REVOKE taxonomy_ro FROM <user>;
\q

Manage Postgres Accounts
Removal steps and Password steps for all Postgres hosts:

To revoke access:
DROP ROLE <user>;
\q
To reset the password for a user:
ALTER USER <user> WITH PASSWORD '<password>';


Want to check if they have an account?
\du <UserName>
# Example usage
# python adtrack.py check kboller@marchex.com
# python adtrack.py grant kboller@marchex.com "Kenneth Boller" --staff
# python adtrack.py remove kboller@marchex.com


from psycopg2 import errors
import logging
import psycopg2
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "..", "Utils"))
from get_secrets import get_secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)


DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack",
    "host": "vspoolint.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": get_secret("_AdTrack_USER"),
    "password": get_secret("_AdTrack_PASS")
}



def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Incorrect User or Password.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    if "@" not in user:
        user_email = f"{user}@marchex.com"
    else:
        user_email = user

    search_param = vendor_email or user_email

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        error_msg = "❌ Database connection failed: Could not establish connection."
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so checkaccess.py captures it
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()

        if result:
            output = f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {result}"
        else:
            output = f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access."

        logging.info(output)
        print(output)  # ✅ Ensure this prints so it's visible in checkaccess.py
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return result

    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"❌ Database query failed: {e}"
        logging.error(error_msg)
        print(error_msg)  # ✅ Ensure errors are visible
        sys.stdout.flush()
        return None

# ✅ GRANT Access Function
def grant_adtrack_access(user_email, is_staff=False):
    """Grants AdTrack UI access by inserting a user into the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        logging.error("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                INSERT INTO at_user (email, status)
                VALUES (%s, 'active')
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

    except psycopg2.errors.UniqueViolation:
        logging.warning(f"User {user_email} already exists in AdTrack. Skipping insert.")
        print(f"⚠️ User {user_email} already exists. No changes made.")

    finally:
        conn.close()
    print(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} in AdTrack.")
    logging.info(f"✅ Granted access to {user_email} (staff={is_staff})")

# ✅ REMOVE Access Function
def remove_adtrack_access(user_email):
    """Disables an AdTrack user's account in the database."""
    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        print("❌ Failed to connect to the AdTrack database.")
        return

    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute("""
                UPDATE at_user
                SET status = 'disabled'
                WHERE email ILIKE %s
            """, (user_email,))
            conn.commit()

        print(f"✅ Removed access for {user_email} in AdTrack.")
        logging.info(f"✅ Disabled access for {user_email}.")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to remove access for {user_email}: {e}")
        print(f"❌ Remove failed for {user_email}: {e}")
    finally:
        conn.close()

# ✅ Main Execution Block
def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python adtrack.py <check|grant|remove> <user> [real_name (if granting)] [--staff]")
        sys.exit(1)

    action = sys.argv[1].lower()
    user = sys.argv[2]
    real_name = sys.argv[3] if len(sys.argv) > 3 else None
    is_staff = "--staff" in sys.argv

    if action == "check":
        check_adtrack_access(user)
    elif action == "grant":
        if not real_name:
            print("❌ Error: Real name required to grant access.")
            sys.exit(1)
        grant_adtrack_access(user, is_staff)

    elif action == "remove":
        remove_adtrack_access(user)
    else:
        print("❌ Invalid action. Use 'check', 'grant', or 'remove'.")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
